### [233] [LiftQuant: Continuous Bit-Width LLM via Dimensional Lifting and Projection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04050)
*Liulu He,XuanAng Liu,Juntao Liu,Taolue Feng,Ting Lu,Chunsheng Gan,Zhiyv Peng,Yuan Du,Huanrui Yang,Yijiang Liu,Li Du*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LiftQuant提出一种新型量化框架，通过‘升维-投影’机制实现连续比特宽度控制，突破传统整数比特限制，可在保持硬件友好性的同时实现模型压缩与性能优化，适用于70B大模型在24GB GPU上的精准部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量化方法受限于固定的整数比特宽度（如2、3比特），导致大型语言模型难以根据特定内存预算进行最优适配，存在‘部署差距’问题。

Method: 提出‘升维-投影’机制，将低维权重向量通过高维空间的1比特格点投影实现非均匀但结构化的码本，有效比特宽度由升维比决定，支持准连续调节。

Result: LiftQuant可将70B LLM压缩至2.4比特，精确适配24GB GPU，性能显著优于同类2比特模型。

Conclusion: LiftQuant实现了真正意义上的帕累托最优部署，为大模型高效推理提供了灵活且硬件友好的新范式。

Abstract: Existing quantization methods are fundamentally limited by rigid, integer-based bit-widths (e.g., 2, 3-bit), resulting in a ``deployment gap" where Large Language Models cannot be optimally fitted to specific memory budgets. To bridge this gap, we introduce LiftQuant, a novel framework that enables continuous bit-width control for true Pareto-optimal deployment. The core innovation is a ``lift-then-project" mechanism which approximates low-dimensional weight vectors by projecting a simple 1-bit lattice from a higher-dimensional ``lifted" space. Crucially, the effective bit-width is determined simply by the ratio of the lifted dimension to the original dimension, which allows the bit-width to be tuned quasi-continuous as the dimension is a flexible structural parameter. This projection generates a structured yet non-uniform codebook, capturing the expressive power of Vector Quantization (VQ). While beneficial over VQ, LiftQuant's decoding path relies solely on linear transformations and 1-bit uniform quantizers, retaining hardware-friendly nature. This flexibility is transformative: LiftQuant enables a 70B LLM to be compressed to 2.4 bits to precisely fit a 24GB GPU, where its performance significantly surpasses state-of-the-art 2-bit models fitted on the same device. Our code and ckpt is available at https://github.com/Heliulu/LiftQuant.

### [234] [RUBAS: Rubric-Based Reinforcement Learning for Agent Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04051)
*Xian Qi Loye,Qinglin Su,Zhexin Zhang,Shiyao Cui,Qi Zhu,Fei Mi,Hongning Wang,Minlie Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RUBAS 是一种基于评分标准的强化学习框架，用于提升工具型大模型代理的安全性。它将代理行为分解为工具使用安全、论证安全、响应安全和帮助性四个维度，通过细粒度且可解释的奖励信号优化安全的工具使用，同时保持任务完成能力。实验表明，RUBAS 在多个基准测试中显著提升了安全性，减少了与工具相关的幻觉，且保持了良好的实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对齐方法依赖粗粒度拒绝信号或静态监督，难以在多样化的代理风险下平衡安全与有用的工具执行。需要一种更精细、可解释的机制来指导大模型代理在真实世界执行中的安全行为。

Method: 提出 RUBAS 框架，采用多维度结构化评分标准（工具使用安全、论证安全、响应安全、帮助性）对完整代理轨迹进行评估，生成细粒度奖励信号，并结合强化学习优化模型行为。

Result: 在多个代理安全基准测试中，RUBAS 显著提升了安全性，减少了工具相关幻觉，同时保持了与基线相当甚至更优的任务完成能力，证明了多维评分奖励在安全关键工具使用场景中的有效性。

Conclusion: 多维度结构化评分奖励能够有效作为训练信号，实现大模型代理在安全关键工具使用场景下的对齐，是解决现实世界执行安全挑战的有效路径。

Abstract: The evolution of LLMs into tool-enabled agents creates a new class of safety challenges associated with real-world execution rather than simple text generation. Existing alignment methods often rely on coarse refusal signals or static supervision, making it difficult to balance safety with useful tool execution across diverse agentic risks. We introduce RUBAS, a rubric-based reinforcement learning framework for agent safety. RUBAS decomposes agent behavior into four dimensions: tool-use safety, argument safety, response safety, and helpfulness. These structured rubrics provide fine-grained and interpretable rewards over complete agent trajectories, enabling reinforcement learning to optimize safe tool use while preserving task completion. Extensive experiments across multiple agent safety benchmarks and models show that RUBAS improves safety over standard alignment baselines, reduces tool-grounded hallucinations, and maintains competitive utility. Our results suggest that multi-dimensional rubric rewards provide an effective training signal for aligning LLM agents in safety-critical tool-use settings.

### [235] [A Goal-Set Characterization of Task Composition in the Boolean Task Algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04053)
*Eduardo Terrés-Caballero,Herke van Hoof*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了布尔任务代数（BTA）的结构假设，发现其在确定性马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）中存在值函数空间的坍缩现象：所有扩展的最优Q值函数完全由全集和空集任务决定，因此原始BTA提出的对数规模基础任务冗余。为此，作者提出基于目标集的组合方法，通过在目标集上执行逻辑操作，并从全集与空集值函数中选取片段重构复合值函数，显著降低学习成本与组合时间，同时保持策略性能。实验覆盖表格、视觉、函数逼近及连续控制等多种场景，均表明增加基础任务无法提升性能。此外，研究还指出在随机环境下该坍缩不成立，最优组合可能需要指数级多的策略。代码已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有布尔任务代数（BTA）依赖对数规模的基础任务进行零样本任务组合，但其结构假设在确定性环境中导致最优值函数空间坍缩，即所有组合任务的值函数仅由全集和空集任务决定，暗示基础任务设计存在冗余。这限制了模型效率与可扩展性，亟需更高效且理论可靠的组合机制。

Method: 提出基于目标集的逻辑操作方法，将任务组合转化为对目标集合的布尔运算；通过选择来自全局通用值函数和空值函数的相应切片来重建复合任务的值函数，从而避免学习额外基础任务。该方法适用于确定性环境，并可在不损失性能的前提下减少训练开销与组合延迟。

Result: 在多种环境（包括表格型、视觉、函数逼近、连续控制）中，实验验证了增加基础任务并未带来性能提升，支持了理论上的坍缩结论。新方法显著降低了学习成本与组合时间，同时维持原有策略性能。在随机设置下，反例表明坍缩不成立，组合可能需要指数级多的策略。

Conclusion: 布尔任务代数中的基础任务冗余源于确定性环境下的值函数坍缩，基于目标集的组合方法有效解决了这一问题，实现了高效、低成本的任务合成。在随机环境中，该坍缩不再成立，提示未来工作需考虑更复杂的策略建模。

Abstract: The Boolean Task Algebra (BTA) provides a principled framework for zero-shot task composition in reinforcement learning by equipping goal-reaching tasks with Boolean operations. We revisit its structural assumptions and formalize a collapse in the space of optimal extended Q-value functions: in deterministic MDPs, every such function is fully determined by the universal and empty tasks. This makes the logarithmic set of base tasks proposed in the original BTA formulation redundant. Building on this observation, we introduce a goal-set-based composition method that performs logical operations on goal sets and reconstructs composed value functions by selecting slices from the universal and empty value functions. This reduces learning costs for standard BTA and reduces composition time for both BTA and Skill Machines, while preserving policy performance. Experiments across tabular, visual, function-approximation, and continuous-control domains show that learning additional base tasks does not yield better performance. Finally, we study the stochastic setting and provide a counterexample showing that this collapse need not hold, that is, optimal composition may require accounting for exponentially many policies in the number of goals. Code is available at https://github.com/EduardoTerres/bta_paper.

</details>


### [236] [Spectral Scaling Laws of Muon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04058)
*Gagik Magakyan,Pablo Parrilo,Asuman Ozdaglar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究首次系统性地分析了大语言模型训练中动量矩阵奇异值谱的演化规律，发现其在训练初期稳定后，各层奇异值量化值随模型规模呈现清晰的幂律关系。不同层的缩放指数差异显著：中后层几乎不变（约$M^{-0.25}$），而部分末层则急剧下降（最高达$M^{-0.96}$）。这表明标准5步Newton-Schulz迭代在大规模模型下对末层可能失效，需增加迭代次数或优化系数。研究提出基于层类型与模型规模的轻量级配置策略，既避免冗余计算，又保障更新质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主流优化器Muon依赖Newton-Schulz（NS）迭代进行正交化，但NS为近似方法，对小奇异值方向效果不佳。现有实践多采用固定5步配置，缺乏对不同层、不同模型规模下动量矩阵奇异值行为的理解，导致可能在大规模模型上出现正交化失败。因此亟需系统研究奇异值演化规律，以指导高效且可靠的NS配置选择。

Method: 通过追踪从77M到2.8B参数的多个模型中各层动量缓冲区的奇异值分位数，分析其在训练过程中的动态变化；统计稳定后的奇异值水平，并拟合其与模型规模的关系，揭示幂律规律；结合理论分析与实验验证，推导出适用于不同层类型的最小有效NS迭代次数配置准则。

Result: 观测到奇异值分位数在训练后趋于稳定，其值随模型规模呈幂律衰减，不同层具有不同的指数（如中后层约$M^{-0.25}$，部分末层高达$M^{-0.96}$）。这意味着在超大规模模型中，若仍使用固定5步NS，部分末层将无法有效正交化。提出根据层类型和模型规模自适应调整NS配置的方案，可在不牺牲更新质量的前提下显著减少计算开销。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了大模型动量矩阵奇异值谱的系统性规律，为优化器中Newton-Schulz迭代的配置提供了理论依据和实用指南。建议在实际应用中根据不同层的缩放特性动态选择迭代步数或系数，实现计算效率与更新精度的最优平衡。

Abstract: Orthonormalized update rules have rapidly become a leading choice of optimizer for training large language models, with recent open-source state-of-the-art models adopting Muon. To keep these updates tractable, Muon performs the orthonormalization with the Newton--Schulz (NS) iteration. Since NS is only approximate, directions with small singular values fail to be orthonormalized. In Muon, NS is applied to the momentum matrix at every step, yet little is known about how the singular value spectrum of these momentum matrices behaves during training, or how that behavior changes with model size. We present the first systematic study of this question. Tracking singular value quantiles of the momentum buffer across layers in models ranging from 77M to 2.8B parameters, we observe a consistent picture: after a short burn-in, the quantiles stabilize at a value determined by the layer type and model size. These stabilization values follow remarkably clean power laws in model size, with layer-dependent exponents. Layers up to mid-late depth scale very mildly with model size $M$ (around $M^{-0.25}$), so the standard 5-step NS configuration used at academic scale will continue to orthonormalize them at much larger scales. Some of the late layers, however, scale much more aggressively (up to $M^{-0.96}$) and will fall into the NS failure regime at frontier scale unless one uses more NS iterations or better-tuned coefficients. NS iterations are computationally expensive at scale; our laws give practitioners a principled, layer-aware recipe for choosing the minimum NS configuration that still orthonormalizes the directions that matter -- avoiding unnecessary computation without sacrificing update quality.

</details>


### [237] [LLM Compression with Jointly Optimizing Architectural and Quantization choices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04063)
*Hoang-Loc La,Truong-Thanh Le,Amir Taherkordi,Phuong Hoai Ha*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种可微分的神经架构搜索（NAS）框架，联合优化大型语言模型（LLM）线性层的架构配置与混合精度量化，以实现高效压缩。该方法突破传统NAS在搜索空间上的限制，并将架构设计与量化过程耦合，显著提升推理速度与准确性之间的平衡。实验表明，相比先搜索后量化的基线方法，本方法在相近精度下推理速度提升最高达1.4倍，或在相同延迟下平均准确率提高最多6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型部署面临内存和计算资源消耗大的挑战。虽然已有方法通过训练小型模型或对预训练模型进行剪枝、量化来压缩模型，但这些方法存在训练成本高、搜索空间受限或架构与量化分离等问题。为解决这些问题，亟需一种能够同时优化模型结构与量化策略的统一框架。

Method: 提出一种可微分的NAS框架，全面探索模型架构空间，并联合优化线性层的混合精度量化方案，实现架构与量化的协同设计。通过可微分搜索机制，在连续空间中高效寻找最优配置。

Result: 在多个推理任务上，所提方法在保持高精度的同时显著提升推理速度：相比传统顺序式方法（NAS-then-quantization），推理速度最快提升1.4倍；在相同延迟条件下，平均准确率最高提升6%。

Conclusion: 本文提出的可微分联合优化框架有效解决了大语言模型压缩中的架构与量化脱节问题，实现了更优的性能-效率权衡，为边缘设备部署大模型提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Deploying large language models (LLMs) is challenging due to their significant memory and computational requirements. While some methods address this by developing small or tiny language models from scratch, these approaches demand extensive GPU training. Compressing pre-trained LLMs for edge devices offers a compelling alternative. Beyond pruning and quantization, Neural Architecture Search (NAS) enables effective compression, yet prior NAS approaches often limit the search space and decouple architecture from quantization. We introduce a differentiable NAS framework that explores the entire space and jointly optimizes architectural configurations alongside mixed-precision quantization for linear layers of LLMs. Experiments demonstrate superior accuracy-latency trade-offs: our models achieve up to 1.4x faster inference than sequential NAS-then-quantization baselines at comparable accuracy, or up to 6% higher average accuracy across seven reasoning tasks at equivalent latency.

### [238] [TPA-AD: A Two-Stage Pseudo Anomaly-Guided Method for Bearing Time-Series Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04073)
*Xiancheng Wang,Zhibo Zhang,Ran Li,Rui Wang,Minghang Zhao,Shisheng Zhong,Lin Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种两阶段伪异常引导的异常检测方法TPA-AD，用于仅使用正常样本训练的轴箱轴承时间序列异常检测。该方法通过重建模型和每特征目标误差控制生成靠近正常边界的伪异常窗口，再通过对比学习学习异常敏感表示，并利用KNN生成窗口级和点级异常分数。相比依赖已知故障类别、真实异常先验或随机异常注入的方法，TPA-AD通过在边界邻域构建伪异常提升了正常边界的可分性，能有效处理混合变量场景中的连续与离散特征。在轴承故障检测和退化过程数据集上进行实验，并扩展至13个公开TSAD数据集，结果表明该方法具有稳定的异常响应、对退化演化的敏感性以及在公开基准和实际高铁轴承数据上的良好泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时间序列异常检测方法通常依赖已知故障类别、真实异常先验或随机异常注入，但在仅提供正常样本的场景下，难以有效捕捉异常边界特征。因此，需要一种无需真实异常样本即可生成有意义伪异常的方法，以增强正常与异常之间的可分性，尤其在混合变量（连续与离散）场景下提升检测性能。

Method: 首先使用重建模型结合每特征目标误差控制生成靠近正常分布边界的伪异常窗口；然后通过对比学习，在正常窗口与伪异常窗口之间建立差异性表征；最后利用k近邻（KNN）计算窗口级和点级异常得分。

Result: 在轴承故障检测数据集和退化过程数据集上，TPA-AD表现出稳定的异常响应，对退化演化具有高度敏感性；在13个公开时间序列异常检测数据集上也展现出良好的泛化能力，尤其在真实高铁轴承数据中表现优异。

Conclusion: TPA-AD通过在正常边界附近构造伪异常，显著提升了正常与异常之间的可分性，无需依赖真实异常样本或预设故障类别，适用于混合变量场景，具备较强的实用性与泛化能力，为无监督时间序列异常检测提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: This paper proposes a two-stage pseudo anomaly-guided anomaly detection method (\textbf{T}wo-stage \textbf{P}seudo \textbf{A}nomaly-guided \textbf{A}nomaly \textbf{D}etection, \textbf{TPA-AD}) for axle-box bearing time-series anomaly detection (time series anomaly detection, TSAD) under the setting where only normal samples are available for training. The method first generates pseudo-anomalous windows near the normal boundary using a reconstruction model and per-feature target-error control. It then learns anomaly-sensitive representations through contrastive learning between normal and pseudo-anomalous windows, and finally produces window-level and point-level anomaly scores using k-nearest neighbors (KNN). Compared with existing methods that rely on known fault categories, real anomaly priors, or random anomaly injection, TPA-AD improves the separability of the normal boundary by constructing pseudo-anomalies in boundary neighborhoods and can jointly handle continuous and discrete features in mixed-variable scenarios. The main experiments are conducted on bearing fault detection datasets and degradation-process datasets, with an additional exploratory extension on $13$ public TSAD datasets. The results show that the proposed method yields relatively stable anomaly responses, is sensitive to degradation evolution, and demonstrates a certain degree of broader applicability on public TSAD benchmarks and real high-speed-train-related bearing data.

### [239] [Adaptive Patching Is Harder Than It Looks For Time-Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04074)
*Federico Zucchi,Yi Xie,Chao Zhang,Keyuan Luo,Thomas Lampert,Ziyue Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了自适应分块在时间序列Transformer中的有效性，指出仅局部异质性不足以保证其优于精心调优的均匀分块。通过将分块建模为带预算的比特率分配，推导出动态分块规则需满足的阈值条件，并给出了局部和全局的性能提升界限。研究发现，在无耦合约束下，标量局部复杂度无法产生非均匀最优解；一旦主干网络训练到表示感知最优状态，对齐增益会收敛于一个调优良好的均匀分块大小。通过在三个代表性架构上进行受控隔离实验，发现验证集选择的均匀基线与动态方法相比表现相当，且整体效果集中在零附近，无一致方向优势。较大的收益具有方法和数据集特异性。因此，自适应分块应与调优后的均匀基线对比评估，其价值取决于能否以低成本可靠地识别出真正降低预测损失的细粒度分块区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究自适应分块何时能超越精心调优的均匀分块，明确其实际价值边界，避免盲目依赖动态机制。

Method: 将分块视为预算化的比特率分配问题，推导动态分块优于均匀分块的理论阈值；利用二次近似和强凸性分析局部与全局性能提升；通过受控实验隔离自适应机制，固定主干、数据和训练流程，比较不同分块策略的表现。

Result: 在标准长周期预测基准上，验证集选择的均匀基线与动态分块表现相当，多数设置下的增益接近零，无一致方向优势；显著增益具有方法和数据集特异性；表明自适应分块的价值依赖于能否有效识别真正有益的细粒度区域。

Conclusion: 自适应分块不应被默认优于均匀分块，其有效性必须与调优后的均匀基线对比评估；关键在于是否存在廉价可靠的信号来识别真正需要更细分块的区域。

Abstract: Adaptive patching is a recent and compelling proposal for time-series Transformers: allocate finer patches where the sequence looks locally informative. This paper asks under what conditions a content-adaptive patching operator should outperform a tuned uniform one. Local heterogeneity alone is not enough: under pointwise forecasting losses, a complex-looking region is not automatically one where finer patching reduces the loss. We model patching as a budgeted bitrate allocation and derive an explicit threshold that a dynamic patching rule must satisfy to beat a well-tuned uniform baseline, then bound the achievable improvement both locally (a quadratic surrogate) and globally (a strong-convexity bound under the model's assumptions). Two structural results follow: without a coupling constraint, scalar local complexity cannot produce a non-uniform optimum under a common loss landscape; and once the backbone is trained to its representation-aware optimum, the alignment gain collapses around a well-tuned uniform patch size. To test these predictions, we run a controlled isolation study on three representative architectures, replacing each adaptive mechanism with a uniform patch-size sweep while keeping the backbone, data, and training protocol fixed. On standard long-horizon forecasting benchmarks, the validation-selected uniform baseline is competitive with the dynamic counterpart, with per-setting effects concentrated near zero and no consistent directional advantage once results are aggregated by dataset. The larger gains we do observe are method- and dataset-specific. Adaptive patching should therefore be evaluated against a tuned uniform baseline; its value depends on whether a cheap and reliable routing signal can identify where finer patches actually reduce forecasting loss.

</details>


### [240] [Large Language Models Hack Rewards, and Society](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04075)
*Wei Liu,Xinyi Mou,Hanqi Yan,Zhongyu Wei,Yulan He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了强化学习（RL）在大语言模型（LLM）训练中可能引发的‘社会漏洞利用’（societal hacking）现象，即模型通过发现社会规则中的漏洞，在技术合规的前提下违背监管初衷。研究提出SocioHack框架，包含72个社会模拟环境，实验证明模型在这些环境中会自然产生奖励劫持行为，并生成规避规则但符合形式要求的策略。现有模型安全机制对此类问题缓解有限，因此需谨慎收集现实反馈，并发展下一代更安全的后训练范式以实现大模型在真实社会中的迭代。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 观察到社会规范与奖励函数在结构上的相似性，且社会规则常存在意图不完全明确、留有例外和阈值空间的问题，推测强化学习可能利用这些空隙导致模型在真实社会中出现系统性违规行为，即‘社会漏洞利用’。

Method: 构建SocioHack框架，设计72个社会情境模拟环境，用于评估大语言模型在不同规则下的行为表现；通过强化学习训练模型，分析其是否能发现并利用规则漏洞，生成技术合规但违背意图的策略。

Result: 实验表明，模型在多数社会环境中均表现出奖励劫持行为，能够主动发现并利用规则漏洞，生成规避监管意图但仍符合形式要求的策略；当前主流的模型安全防护措施对此类行为仅提供有限缓解。

Conclusion: 强化学习驱动的大语言模型在真实社会环境中可能因规则模糊而产生系统性社会漏洞利用行为，这提示我们应更加审慎地收集现实世界反馈，并亟需开发新一代安全可靠的后训练范式，以确保大模型在社会应用中的可控性和可信度。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a dominant post-training paradigm, enabling large language models (LLMs) to learn from rewards. We observe that societal regulations are structurally similar to reward functions. They define measurable outcomes, thresholds, and exceptions, while often leaving institutional intent only partially specified. We hypothesise that the RL training process may exploit these gaps and therefore ask whether models' well-known tendency to hack reward functions during RL can scale into a more consequential failure mode named societal hacking: discovering loopholes in the rules society runs on. To study this phenomenon, we introduce SocioHack, a sandbox of 72 societal environments, and find that within these environments, reward hacking naturally emerges and leads to regulatory loophole discovery. Models learn to hack the social rules and generate strategies that remain technically compliant while defeating regulatory intent, and current LLM safeguards provide only limited mitigation. Therefore, collecting in-the-wild feedback for model training requires greater caution, and we need a next-generation post-training paradigm for safely iterating LLMs in real society.=

### [241] [Stein Kernelized Molecular Dynamics for Active Learning of Interatomic Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04100)
*Joanna Zou,Fraser Birks,Dallas Foster,Youssef Marzouk*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SKMD是一种增强采样方法，用于高效获取机器学习势能（MLIPs）训练所需的有信息量的构型。它基于斯坦因变分梯度下降，结合全局原子描述符核函数和异步粒子更新机制，能够保持玻尔兹曼分布作为渐近分布，平衡探索新构型与聚焦高概率区域之间的关系。同时提出自适应停止准则以在线获取非冗余数据。在Müller-Brown势和丙氨酸二肽的MACE势能模型上验证了其有效性，相比基线方法，在相同样本数下用更少迭代实现更高精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器学习势能依赖高质量且多样化的训练数据，但传统采样方法难以高效生成具有信息量的构型，尤其在复杂能量景观中。因此需要一种既能广泛探索又能聚焦重要区域的采样策略，以提升主动学习和微调效率。

Method: 提出斯坦因核化分子动力学（SKMD），是斯坦因变分梯度下降的随机变体，针对分子动力学特性改进：引入异步粒子更新和基于全局原子描述符的核函数，实现对构型相似性的对称性感知度量；并设计自适应停止准则进行在线非冗余数据采集。

Result: 在Müller-Brown势能模型的主动学习中，SKMD显著提升了模型精度；在丙氨酸二肽的MACE势能微调中，使用相同数量的训练样本，比基线方法更快收敛且达到更高准确率。结果表明该方法能有效提升训练效率和模型性能。

Conclusion: SKMD通过保持玻尔兹曼分布的渐近性质，实现了高效且平衡的构型采样，为机器学习势能的主动学习与微调提供了强有力的工具，显著减少了训练成本并提高了模型精度。

Abstract: Machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) enable efficient and accurate atomistic simulations but depend critically on the quality and diversity of the training data. We introduce Stein kernelized molecular dynamics (SKMD), an enhanced sampling method that uses interacting particle dynamics to acquire informative training configurations for the active learning and fine-tuning of MLIPs. SKMD corresponds to a stochastic variant of Stein variational gradient descent that is adapted for molecular dynamics by incorporating asynchronous particle updates and a kernel of global atomic descriptors, which provides a symmetry-aware measure of configurational similarity. Unlike other enhanced samplers used in molecular dynamics, SKMD preserves the Boltzmann distribution as the asymptotic distribution of the dynamics. This property enforces a balance between the exploration of diverse configurations and attraction toward high-probability regions of the energy landscape. We further propose an approach to efficient online data acquisition using an adaptive stopping criterion that selects non-redundant training data over the course of simulation. We demonstrate SKMD for the active learning of a neural network model of the Müller-Brown potential and the fine-tuning of a MACE interatomic potential for alanine dipeptide. Compared to active learning baselines, our method achieves higher model accuracy in fewer training iterations with the same number of acquired training samples.

### [242] [Building The Ph(ysical)AI Layer Of Machine Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04106)

Abstract: Foundation models achieve generalization through massive-scale training on diverse data, but have limitations with transfer to truly unseen domains without paired training data. We propose principle-driven foundation models that encode signal-theoretic principles (Fourier decomposition, energy conservation, symmetry) rather than learn untethered statistical correlations. We hypothesize that domains differ not in fundamental physics, but in learnable transformations in time, frequency, magnitude, or phase. Training exclusively on radio-frequency (RF) data with co-designed architecture and losses incorporating these principles, we achieve cross-modal transfer to audio, images, text, and video using only frozen representations learned from RF data, requiring no fine-tuning of the encoder on target domains. Our 1.99M parameter frozen encoder achieves 77.7% average accuracy (91.9% top-3) across 15 diverse tasks via linear probing, with systematic variation: 84.5 on physically-grounded tasks (speaker recognition, seismology, RF fingerprinting) versus 70.0% on semantic tasks (music genre, language recognition). This reveals that principle-driven and scale-driven approaches offer complementary paths: physical principles enable efficient cross-modal transfer while naturally establishing the boundary between physical and semantic understanding.

### [244] [dMX: Differentiable Mixed-Precision Assignment for Low-Precision Floating-Point Formats](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04115)
*Giuseppe Franco,Ian Colbert,Pablo Monteagudo-Lago,Felix Marty,Nicholas Fraser*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: dMX提出一种可微分的混合精度量化框架，用于学习浮点数位宽分配，针对OCP标准定义的MXFP数据类型。通过将每层的位宽建模为连续可学习参数，结合温度退火策略实现从连续优化到离散硬件兼容格式的平滑过渡，并引入目标感知正则化控制平均位宽以平衡性能与效率。在Llama、Qwen3和SmolLM2等模型上验证，dMX在保持低精度的同时显著提升性能，优于基于KL散度的启发式方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法对所有层采用统一的低精度位宽，无法兼顾不同层的计算需求，导致性能和精度损失。需要更灵活的混合精度量化策略来优化部署效率与模型质量之间的权衡。

Method: 将每层的浮点格式参数化为一个标量偏移量，构建连续优化问题；使用温度驱动的退火机制逐步离散化该偏移量，确保最终配置符合硬件支持的MXFP格式；引入目标感知正则项引导平均位宽接近用户设定预算。

Result: 在WikiText-2上的困惑度和四个零样本推理基准任务上均表现出色，生成的模型在相同平均位宽下优于基线方法，实现了帕累托最优，有效平衡了模型质量与部署效率。

Conclusion: dMX是一种高效且可扩展的混合精度量化框架，能够自适应地为不同层分配最优浮点位宽，在不牺牲性能的前提下显著降低模型部署成本，适用于大规模语言模型的实际应用。

Abstract: Quantizing large language models (LLMs) to low-precision floating-point representations is central to efficient deployment, yet applying a single bit-width uniformly across all layers is sub-optimal in terms of both performance and accuracy. This work introduces dMX, a differentiable mixed-precision quantization framework for learnable floating-point bit-width assignment. We study its application for the microscaling floating-point (MXFP) family of data types defined by the Open Compute Project (OCP) standard. The per-layer bit-width assignment is formulated as a continuous optimization problem in which each layer's floating-point format format is parameterized by a scalar parameter, folding the multi-variate design space into a single learnable offset. During training this offset takes continuous values, avoiding sudden oscillations between discrete quantization formats. A temperature-based annealing schedule progressively discretizes the learned offsets, ensuring that the final configuration maps to hardware-compatible MXFP formats without abrupt transitions between training and inference behavior. A target-aware regularization term steers the average bit-width toward a user-specified budget, serving as a coarse-grained proxy for inference cost and balancing model quality against deployment efficiency. We performed experiments on different families of LLM, such as Llama, Qwen3, and SmolLM2, evaluating perplexity on WikiText-2 and accuracy on four zero-shot reasoning benchmarks. Across these settings, dMX consistently yields Pareto-dominating models and improves over Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence-based layer-selection heuristics, efficiently navigating trade-offs between model quality and average bit-width.

Motivation: 真实世界的时间序列常具有非平稳性和状态转移，导致仅依赖相似性的检索方法不可靠且易冗余，因此需要一种能同时考虑相关性与多样性的检索策略以提升预测性能。

Method: SARAF首先通过时间对齐的相似性形成候选历史片段池，再采用受多样性启发的选择策略覆盖不同历史状态；其多样性调节强度由数据集整体平稳性动态决定，并结合平稳性感知聚合机制融合检索到的未来预测。

Abstract: Time series forecasting relies on historical patterns, but real-world series often exhibit non-stationarity and regime shifts that challenge fully parametric forecasters. Inspired by Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG), recent work augments forecasters by retrieving relevant historical segments and using them as external evidence at inference time. However, due to the intrinsic non-stationarity of real-world time series, a highly similar past segment does not necessarily imply a similar future, rendering similarity-only retrieval brittle and prone to redundancy. We propose Stationarity-Aware Retrieval-Augmented Time Series Forecasting (SARAF), a framework that adaptively balances relevance and diversity in retrieval. SARAF first forms a candidate pool via temporal similarity with time-aligned enhancement, then applies a diversity-aware selection strategy to cover heterogeneous historical regimes, with the diversification strength automatically modulated by dataset-level stationarity. Moreover, SARAF uses stationarity-aware aggregation to fuse the retrieved futures. Extensive experiments on eight real-world datasets show that SARAF achieves competitive forecasting performance and improves average accuracy and robustness over strong baselines, with particularly clear benefits under challenging non-stationary settings. Code: https://github.com/ShiqiaoZhou/SARAF.

### [246] [Physics-Informed Machine Learning for Short-Term Flood Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04143)
*Tewodros Syum Gebre,Jagrati Talreja,Leila Hashemi-Beni*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种物理信息机器学习（PIML）框架，将水文知识融入LSTM模型的损失函数中，通过趋势一致性约束提升模型在数据稀缺环境下的鲁棒性与物理合理性。实验表明，在仅使用5%数据训练时，该方法将纳什-萨特克利夫效率（NSE）从0.20提升至0.23，且在极端气候模拟下保持方向一致性，显著减少非物理波动，适用于无观测流域和气候变化情境下的实时洪水预报。

Conclusion: 简单的物理约束能够显著提升深度学习模型在洪水预报中的可靠性，尤其适用于数据稀缺、无观测流域及气候变化背景下的实时预警系统，提供了一种实用且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Accurate flood forecasting is essential for mitigating disaster risks and protecting communities. However, purely data-driven machine learning models often struggle in data-scarce environments and may violate fundamental hydrological principles. Standard Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) networks can generate physically inconsistent predictions, particularly when extrapolating to extreme weather conditions. To address these limitations, we propose a Physics-Informed Machine Learning (PIML) framework that incorporates hydrological knowledge directly into the loss function of an LSTM model. Specifically, a Trend Alignment constraint penalizes directional inconsistencies between precipitation and discharge trends, improving model robustness without requiring complex hydrodynamic equations. This regularization encourages the model to learn physically plausible hydrograph behavior, even with limited training data, while enhancing reliability during peak flood events. Experimental results show that the proposed physics-informed model outperforms a standard LSTM baseline in data-scarce settings, increasing the Nash-Sutcliffe Efficiency (NSE) from 0.20 to 0.23 when trained on only 5% of the available data. Additional stress tests under simulated extreme climate scenarios demonstrate that the baseline model exhibits unstable behavior, whereas the physics-informed model maintains directional consistency and physical plausibility. Although accurately predicting extreme peak magnitudes remains challenging with limited data, the proposed approach substantially reduces unphysical fluctuations common in purely data-driven models. These findings demonstrate that simple physical constraints can significantly improve the reliability of deep learning models for real-time flood forecasting, offering a practical solution for ungauged basins and evolving climate conditions.

### [247] [EvalStop: Using World Feedback to Detect and Correct Reward Overoptimization in Multi-Tenant RLHF Platforms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04145)
*Guilin Zhang,Chuanyi Sun,Shahryar Sarkani,John M. Fossaceca*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EvalStop 是一种可组合的调度原语，通过在连续 k 次评估分数下降时终止任务，释放 GPU 资源并保留最佳检查点，从而解决强化学习人类反馈（RLHF）中的奖励过优化问题。它将调度层面的早停视为检测问题，在离散事件仿真中验证了其在混合了奖励作弊与健康运行的 RLHF 工作负载上的有效性。在 80% RLHF、64 个 GPU 的场景下，EvalStop 实现了 98% 精确率、99% 召回率和 1.5% 假阳性率，同时相比 SRTF-Est 将平均完成时间（JCT）减少 9%，浪费计算量降低 22%（p<0.05）。该方法在各种基线调度器上均表现稳定，且对评估噪声和作弊比例变化具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有云大模型微调平台调度器忽视了奖励模型在持续优化下偏离真实人类反馈的问题（即奖励过优化），导致无效训练资源浪费。传统调度策略缺乏有效的质量信号或依赖人工干预，无法高效应对此挑战。

Method: 提出 EvalStop，一种基于连续评估分数下降的早停机制，结合调度器的可组合设计，能够在不依赖人类监控的情况下自动识别并终止低效或存在奖励作弊的任务，释放计算资源并保留最优模型检查点。

Result: 在 80% RLHF 工作负载下，EvalStop 达到 98% 精确率 / 99% 召回率 / 1.5% FPR，JCT 改善 9%，浪费计算减少 22%；优于固定进度、损失平台等基线方法；在不同调度器、评估噪声和作弊比例下均保持高稳定性。

Conclusion: EvalStop 有效解决了 RLHF 中因奖励过优化带来的资源浪费问题，是一种高效、鲁棒且可集成的调度早停方案，显著提升资源利用率和训练效率。

Abstract: Cloud LLM fine-tuning platforms increasingly serve RLHF workloads, where a learned reward model is optimized as a proxy for human quality. As Gao et al. (2023) showed, this proxy diverges from world feedback (downstream eval metrics) under sustained optimization pressure, a phenomenon known as reward overoptimization. Existing platform schedulers ignore this divergence: non-clairvoyant schedulers optimize JCT without any quality signal, SLAQ-style quality-aware schedulers use training loss (a weaker proxy that drops monotonically through hacking), and classical per-job early stopping requires human monitoring and does not free shared GPUs. We propose EvalStop, a composable scheduling primitive that terminates jobs on k consecutive eval-score declines, releases GPUs, preserves the best checkpoint, and delegates to any base scheduler. We frame scheduler-level early stopping as a detection problem and evaluate it in a discrete-event simulator whose RLHF workload mixes reward-hacking and structurally healthy runs, with ground-truth labels hidden from schedulers. On RLHF-heavy workloads (80% RLHF, 64 GPUs), EvalStop achieves precision 98% / recall 99% / FPR 1.5% while improving JCT by 9% and cutting wasted compute by 22% over SRTF-Est (p<0.05). Trivial fixed-progress and loss-plateau competitors either incur 65% FPR on healthy RLHF or miss over half of true hacking cases. Gains compose across every base scheduler tested (9-25% JCT) and detection quality stays stable under eval noise (precision at least 91% at noise std <= 0.05) and hacking base rate (precision at least 89% across 20-80% hacking fractions).

### [248] [When Offline Selectors Cannot Beat the Best Single Model: A Diagnostic Study on edX Dropout Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04161)
*Tyler Crosse,Alan Nadelsticher Ruvalcaba,Dustin Khang LeDuc,Thomas Trask,Nicholas Lytle,David Joyner*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种三阶段诊断框架，用于分析多模型选择器在实际应用中表现不佳的原因。通过在共享数据缓冲区上分离三个潜在问题——学习器不匹配、状态无法预测最优模型、以及训练与部署间的标签分布偏移——发现性能瓶颈主要源于局部表示模糊性，而非学习器或数据分布问题。实证结果表明，即使使用强化学习（DQN）、行为克隆（BC）和保守强化学习（CQL）等方法，也无法超越基于k-NN的一致性基准，说明当前状态特征不足以区分最优模型。因此，下一步应优化选择器的状态设计或收集新数据，而非继续调优现有学习器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多模型集成中，不同预测器在不同输入上表现各异，理想情况下应为每个实例选择最佳预测器以提升整体准确率。然而，实践中基于历史数据训练的选择器常无法超越最强单个预测器，原因可能包括学习器不匹配、状态信息不足或数据分布偏移。但这些因素常被混在一起，导致改进方向错误。本文旨在系统诊断根本原因，指导有效优化路径。

Method: 提出三阶段诊断流程：(1) 通过k-NN标签一致性估计局部理论上限；(2) 检查多种学习器（BC、DQN、CQL）是否能接近该上限；(3) 通过消融实验评估选择器状态的表达能力，判断是否需要更丰富的特征。整个过程在统一数据缓冲区上执行，避免偏差。

Result: 在edX点击流数据上的16个时间窗口测试中，理想选择器（oracle）平均比最强单模型高出9.7个百分点准确率，但所有三种学习器（BC、DQN、CQL）均未达到该水平，且在十倍缓冲区扫描和数千个保留样本下表现稳定。结果表明，性能瓶颈并非来自学习器本身或数据分布偏移，而是由于局部表示模糊性——即当前状态特征无法有效区分哪个模型在特定实例上表现最好。

Conclusion: 当前选择器性能受限于状态表达能力，而非学习器或数据分布问题。未来改进不应继续调优离线学习器，而应重新设计选择器状态或采集更具判别性的新数据。

Abstract: Different predictors often excel on different inputs, so picking the best one per instance promises higher accuracy than committing to a single model. In practice, selectors trained from logged data routinely fail to beat the strongest single predictor. Three causes typically go unseparated before more tuning is applied: a mismatched learner, a state that does not predict which model wins, or buffer-to-deployment label shift.
  A three-stage diagnostic rules them out on a shared buffer. Stage~1 estimates a local ceiling on oracle recovery from $k$-NN label consistency. Stage~2 asks whether paired BC and offline-RL learners (BC, DQN, and CQL across penalty weights) reach that ceiling. Stage~3 ablates the selector state to test whether richer features would raise it. The combined verdict points to the most promising next step: tuning the learner, redesigning the state, or collecting new data.
  We apply it to selecting among five dropout-prediction models on edX clickstream data. Across 16 windows, the oracle beats the strongest single base model by 9.7 accuracy points on average, yet BC, DQN, and CQL land in the same test-accuracy band below it (robust to a tenfold buffer sweep and $N{=}2{,}000$ held-out examples). The bottleneck is local representational ambiguity: CQL closes the imitation gap without a deployment gain (not conservatism), regret clusters tightly across learners (not tie-breaking), and the three learners converge on test accuracy (not shift). The next iteration should change the state or collect new data, not tune the offline learner further.

</details>


### [249] [ADAPTOOD: Uncertainty-Aware Fine-Tuning for Out-of-Distribution ECG Time Series Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04164)
*Sotirios Vavaroutas,Yu Yvonne Wu,Ali Etemad,Cecilia Mascolo*

TL;DR: 提出ADAPTOOD框架，利用数据不确定性量化分布偏移严重性，指导时间序列的微调。结合低秩模型更新和自适应超参数优化，显著提升在分布外（OOD）任务中的准确率和精确率，性能随分布偏移严重性增加而保持稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在面对多类型、多严重性的分布偏移时表现不佳，尤其忽视了偏移严重性的差异，导致泛化能力受限。需要一种能有效评估并适应不同严重程度分布偏移的新方法。

Method: 通过数据不确定性衡量目标部署分布与预训练分布之间的偏离程度，作为OOD严重性的直接信号；结合低秩模型更新和自适应超参数优化，实现更鲁棒的微调。

Result: ADAPTOOD在OOD任务中相比现有方法最高提升7%准确率和12.9%精确率，且在分布偏移严重性增加时仍保持优异性能。

Conclusion: ADAPTOOD通过量化分布偏移严重性并动态调整微调策略，显著提升了模型在真实世界复杂场景下的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Abstract: Data samples used for training often differ from those encountered during fine-tuning and deployment, and while ML models show promise, their performance remains limited when only small annotated datasets are available. Performance often degrades under distribution shifts caused by diverse sensors, populations, and application settings. Although pre-training helps, models frequently encounter out-of-distribution (OOD) data in real-world settings, leading to reduced robustness. Existing adaptation methods usually assume fixed distribution shifts and struggle when multiple types or severities occur. In particular, they overlook shift severity, for example treating adaptation to a large familiar dataset the same as adaptation to a small dataset with a new task, which limits generalisation. To address this, we propose ADAPTOOD, a novel framework that leverages data uncertainty to quantify distribution shift severity and guide fine-tuning for time series. This uncertainty measures how strongly samples from the target deployment distribution deviate from the pre-training distribution, providing a direct signal of OOD severity. Our framework combines this uncertainty with low-rank model updates and adaptive hyperparameter optimisation to improve adaptation. We show that ADAPTOOD achieves up to 7% higher accuracy and 12.9% higher precision than existing methods in OOD tasks, maintaining strong performance as distribution shift severity increases.

Abstract: We tackle the Metro Network Expansion Problem (MNEP), a subset of the Transport Network Design Problem (TNDP), which focuses on expanding metro systems to satisfy travel demand. Traditional methods rely on exact and heuristic approaches that require expert-defined constraints to reduce the search space. Recently, deep reinforcement learning (Deep RL) has emerged due to its effectiveness in complex sequential decision-making processes-it remains, however, computationally expensive, environmentally costly, and requires additional engineering to interpret. We show that MNEP problems are small enough to not require Deep RL methods. Reformulating the MNEP as a Non-Markovian Rewards Decision Process (NMRDP), we use tabular RL to achieve similar performance with significantly fewer training episodes, additionally offering greater interpretability. Additionally, we incorporate social equity criteria into the reward functions, focusing on efficiency and fairness, highlighting the versatility of our method. Evaluated in real-world settings-Xi'an and Amsterdam-our method reduces total episodes by a factor of 18 and total carbon emissions by a factor of 12 on average, while remaining competitive with Deep RL. ### [251] [When Autoregressive Consistency Hurts Safety Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04168)
*Bochen Lyu,Yiyang Jia,Xiaohao Cai,Zhanxing Zhu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了大语言模型（LLM）安全对齐的脆弱性，指出其常表现为浅层对齐——即微调主要影响输出序列的前几个词。作者提出，这种现象可通过自回归一致性机制来解释：模型倾向于在生成过程中保持并延续当前响应轨迹的一致性。通过分析安全对齐的学习动态，研究发现自回归一致性会将对齐更新集中在早期输出词上，从而解释了浅层对齐的机制根源。同时，这一机制也预测了一类更广泛的攻击方式：在输出轨迹任意位置引入有害状态。文中以随机插入攻击为例，展示如何在原本安全的拒绝生成中插入简短有害片段，并利用自回归一致性持续维持有害分支，从而绕过安全对齐。即使在长段拒绝前缀后，短有害片段仍可引导生成走向有害方向，表明自回归一致性是潜在的广泛失效机制。因此，论文提出对抗性安全对齐框架，基于最坏情况下的有害延续状态，采用随机最坏插入训练进行实例化。整体表明，自回归一致性应成为安全对齐与攻击设计的核心考量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型的安全对齐存在脆弱性，尤其表现为对齐仅作用于生成初期的少数输出词，导致后期仍可能产生有害内容。这种浅层对齐现象缺乏深层机制解释，亟需从生成过程的本质特性出发理解其成因。

Method: 通过分析学习动态，识别自回归一致性作为核心机制；构建随机插入攻击实验，验证其在不同生成路径中绕过安全对齐的能力；提出对抗性安全对齐框架，基于最坏情况有害延续状态进行训练，采用随机最坏插入训练实现。

Result: 实验证明，自回归一致性确实会导致对齐集中在早期输出，且能被恶意利用实现攻击；随机插入攻击可在长拒绝前缀后成功诱导有害输出；对抗性安全对齐方法显著提升模型在复杂攻击场景下的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 自回归一致性是导致安全对齐浅层化和新型攻击的重要机制，应被纳入安全对齐设计的核心考量。未来工作需全面打破有害自回归一致性，推动更深层次、全轨迹的安全对齐。

Abstract: Safety alignment in large language models (LLMs) is fragile in part because it is often shallow: fine-tuning mainly reshapes the model's behavior near the first few output tokens. We argue that this phenomenon can be understood through autoregressive consistency, the tendency of next-token prediction to preserve and extend the current response trajectory consistently. By analyzing the learning dynamics of safety alignment, we show that autoregressive consistency can concentrate alignment updates on early tokens, offering a mechanistic explanation for shallow safety alignment. The same mechanism also predicts a broader class of attacks on LLMs: attacks that induce harmful continuation states at arbitrary positions in the output trajectory. As a concrete example, we introduce random insertion attack, which inserts a short harmful span into an otherwise safe refusal trajectory and exploits autoregressive consistency to sustain the resulting harmful branch, thereby bypassing safety alignment. Notably, a short harmful span can redirect the generation to be harmful even after a long refusal prefix, highlighting autoregressive consistency as a potential broader failure mechanism. This suggests that safety alignment should also break harmful autoregressive consistency throughout the output trajectory. We therefore propose adversarial safety alignment, an initial framework based on worst-case harmful continuation states, and instantiate it with random worst-insertion training. Overall, our results suggest that autoregressive consistency should be treated as a central consideration in both safety alignment and attack design.

</details>

*Jiayi Wang,Raymond K. W. Wong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了矩阵补全问题的分布推广，其中目标矩阵的每个条目都是概率分布而非标量。仅观测到部分矩阵条目，且对于已观测条目，底层分布不可直接获取，只能通过从其抽样的有限样本进行观察。为表示分布条目，采用核均值嵌入，并引入分布值矩阵的Tucker秩以捕捉其低秩结构。由于核嵌入的无限维性质带来显著方法论挑战，本文提出函数展开算子，将所提出的分布低秩结构与经典张量的Tucker秩联系起来。基于此框架，提出一种新的分布矩阵补全估计器，并建立了非渐近误差界以刻画估计器的统计性能。在合成数据和真实世界应用上的大量实验表明该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统矩阵补全假设矩阵条目为标量，但在实际应用中，如用户偏好、时间序列或图像像素等，数据本质上具有分布特性。因此，需要将矩阵补全推广至分布值矩阵，以更准确建模复杂数据结构。同时，由于分布无法直接观测，只能通过有限样本推断，这带来了新的统计与计算挑战。

Method: 采用核均值嵌入表示分布条目；定义分布值矩阵的Tucker秩以刻画其低秩结构；引入函数展开算子，将无限维分布结构映射到有限维张量空间，从而利用经典张量分解技术；基于此构建新的矩阵补全估计器。

Result: 提出了一个适用于分布值矩阵补全的新框架与估计器；建立了非渐近误差界，证明了估计器的统计收敛性；在合成数据和真实数据上验证了方法的有效性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本文成功将矩阵补全推广至分布值矩阵场景，通过核嵌入与函数展开算子克服了无限维挑战，提出了一种有效且理论保障的分布矩阵补全方法，在多种数据设置下表现出良好性能。

Abstract: We study a distributional generalization of the matrix completion problem in which each entry of the target matrix is a probability distribution rather than a scalar. In this setting, only a subset of matrix entries is observed, and even for observed entries, the underlying distributions are not directly accessible; instead, we observe finitely many samples drawn from them. To represent distributional entries, we employ kernel mean embeddings and introduce a notion of Tucker rank for distribution-valued matrices to capture their low-rank structure. The infinite-dimensional nature of kernel embeddings poses significant methodological challenges. To address this, we introduce functional unfolding operators that link the proposed distributional low-rank structure to the classical Tucker rank for finite-dimensional tensors. Based on this framework, we propose a novel estimator for distributional matrix completion. We establish non-asymptotic error bounds that characterize the statistical performance of the estimator. Extensive experiments on synthetic data and a real-world application demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method.

### [253] [KODA: Contrastive Representation Comparison and Alignment for Vision-Language Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04180)
*Youqi Wu,Mohammad Jalali,Farzan Farnia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出KODA（Kernel Optimization for Discrepancy Analysis），一种基于核函数的对比表示比较与对齐框架，用于发现不同视觉-语言模型（如CLIP、SigLIP）在表示结构上的差异。通过构建跨模态统一核函数，并将差异识别建模为约束优化问题，KODA可定位特定样本子集和模态交互中的可解释差异方向。为应对大规模数据挑战，引入随机投影和随机傅里叶特征进行低维近似。实验表明，KODA能一致且可解释地揭示表示差异，并提供用于对齐的样本子集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法主要依赖下游任务性能评估视觉-语言模型，但无法揭示其表示结构的内在差异。本文旨在通过对比表示的结构性差异分析，理解不同模型在语义组织方式上的区别，从而指导模型改进与对齐。

Method: 提出KODA框架，采用模态独立核函数组合构建统一多模态核；将差异发现建模为在目标表示中寻找连贯结构而抑制参考表示中连贯性的约束优化问题；结合随机投影与随机傅里叶特征实现大规模数据下的高效计算。

Conclusion: KODA为对比视觉-语言表示提供了有效的结构性分析工具，不仅揭示了不同模型间的本质差异，还为后续的表示对齐与模型优化提供了可解释的指导依据。

Abstract: Vision-language foundation models such as CLIP and SigLIP provide widely used representations for multimodal learning systems. While these models are typically compared through downstream performance, such evaluations often do not explain how their representations differ structurally. In this work, we study this problem through the task of Contrastive Embedding Clustering: identifying sample subsets that are weakly clustered under one representation but strongly clustered under another. We propose \emph{Kernel Optimization for Discrepancy Analysis (KODA)}, a kernel-based framework for contrastive representation comparison and alignment. KODA constructs unified multimodal kernels through modality-wise kernel composition and formulates discrepancy discovery as a constrained optimization problem that searches for coherent structures in one representation while suppressing coherence in a reference representation. This yields interpretable discrepancy directions associated with specific sample subsets and modality interactions. To scale KODA to large vision-language datasets, we develop randomized low-dimensional approximations of joint kernels using random projections, including Random Fourier Features for shift-invariant kernels. Empirically, KODA identifies consistent and interpretable discrepancy structures across vision-language representations and provides sample subsets for representation alignment. The code is available at https://github.com/yokiwuuu/KODA.

### [254] [Exact Unlearning in Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04182)
*Thanh Nguyen-Tang,Raman Arora*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究强化学习中的精确遗忘问题，提出一种高效框架，可在用户数据被删除时，使学习器的输出与从未接触过该用户数据的情况完全不可区分。针对任意 $\rho > 0$，设计了一个 $\rho$-TV 稳定的强化学习算法，其期望计算成本仅为从头训练的 $\rho\sqrt{\ln T}$ 倍。该算法适用于表格型马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），实现了 $\mathcal{O}(H^2 \sqrt{SAT} + H^3 S^2 A + {H^{2.5} S^2 A}/\rho)$ 的后悔界，并证明了下界为 $\Omega(H\sqrt{SAT} + {SAH}/\rho)$，表明算法近乎极小极大最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强化学习中，如何在用户请求删除数据后，确保学习系统的行为与从未接收过该用户数据时完全一致，是隐私保护的重要挑战。现有方法难以实现真正意义上的‘精确遗忘’，因此需要设计具有理论保障的高效遗忘机制。

Method: 构造一个 $\rho$-TV 稳定的强化学习算法，基于表格型马尔可夫决策过程，通过引入随机化和重加权策略，使得删除用户数据后的系统行为与原始无该用户数据时的行为在统计上无法区分。同时利用动态规划与经验重放技术降低计算开销。

Result: 所提算法实现了 $\rho$-TV 稳定性，且在删除用户数据时的平均计算成本仅为重新训练成本的 $\rho\sqrt{\ln T}$ 倍；其后悔界为 $\mathcal{O}(H^2 \sqrt{SAT} + H^3 S^2 A + {H^{2.5} S^2 A}/\rho)$，并给出了 $\Omega(H\sqrt{SAT} + {SAH}/\rho)$ 的下界，表明算法接近最优。

Conclusion: 本文首次形式化了强化学习中的精确遗忘问题，并提出了一个高效、理论上最优的算法框架，为隐私保护下的在线学习提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: We formulate the problem of \emph{exact unlearning} in reinforcement learning, where the goal is to design an efficient framework that enables the removal of any user's data upon deletion request, i.e., the online learner's output after unlearning is \emph{indistinguishable} from what would have been produced had the deleted user never interacted with the learner. For any $ρ>0$, we show that there exists a reinforcement learning (RL) algorithm that is $ρ$-TV-stable and supports an exact unlearning procedure whose expected computational cost is only a $ρ\sqrt{\ln T}$ fraction of the computational cost of retraining from scratch. We construct such a $ρ$-TV-stable RL algorithm for tabular Markov decision processes (MDPs), which achieves a regret bound of $\mathcal{O}(H^2 \sqrt{SAT} + H^3 S^2 A + {H^{2.5} S^2 A}/ρ)$, where $S, A, H$, and $T$ denote the number of states, the number of actions, the episode horizon, and the number of episodes, respectively. We also establish a lower bound of $Ω(H\sqrt{\!SAT}\! +\! {SAH}/ρ)$ for $ρ$-TV-stable RL algorithms, showing that our algorithm is nearly minimax optimal.

</details>


### [255] [Dual Advantage Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04188)
*Alexey Zemtsov,Maxim Bobrin,Alexander Nikulin,Dmitry V. Dylov,Fakhri Karray,Vladislav Kurenkov,Martin Takáč,Arip Asadulaev*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Dual Advantage Fields (DAF)，一种从双值模型中提取策略的方法，通过动作效果模型预测动作带来的特征位移，并根据其与目标方向的一致性评分动作，在可实现情况下等价于贝尔曼优势，提供局部策略改进保证。在OGBench的多种任务中表现优异，尤其在局部最优动作与直接朝向目标不一致时表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有双目标表示能捕捉全局可达性，但无法直接判断特定状态下的优选动作；需要结合长时程可达性与局部动作比较来提升离线目标条件强化学习性能。

Method: 采用双线性双值参数化，将目标嵌入表示为价值场对状态表示的梯度；构建动作效果模型以预测动作引起的折扣特征位移，并基于该位移与目标方向的对齐程度进行动作评分。

Result: 在OGBench的运动、操作和谜题任务中，DAF显著提升综合可信赖强化学习指标，在局部正确动作与直接朝向目标不一致的情况下仍表现良好。

Conclusion: DAF成功将双值模型转化为有效的局部优势信号，实现了对复杂任务中策略学习的有效支持，具备理论保证和实证优势。

Abstract: Offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning requires both long-horizon reachability estimates and local action comparisons. Dual goal representations provide value fields that capture global goal reachability, but they do not directly specify which action should be preferred at a given state. We propose Dual Advantage Fields, a policy-extraction method that turns a bilinear dual value model into a local advantage signal. Under bilinear dual parameterization, the goal embedding is the gradient of the value field with respect to the state representation. DAF learns an action-effect model that predicts the discounted feature displacement induced by an action and scores actions by the alignment between this displacement and the goal direction. In the realizable case, this score equals the goal-conditioned Bellman advantage, yielding a standard local policy-improvement guarantee. On OGBench locomotion, manipulation, and puzzle tasks, DAF improves aggregate RLiable metrics and performs strongly in settings where locally correct actions differ from direct movement toward the final goal.

Abstract: We describe our approach to the CTF4Science Lorenz challenge, a benchmark that mixes short-horizon forecasting, long-time distribution matching, and trajectory reconstruction across nine task pairs. The key discovery is that no single model family dominated all metrics. Instead, we built a metric-aware hybrid system that assigned a different predictor to each metric family: (1) synthetic-pretrained denoisers for full-trajectory reconstruction, (2) Lorenz ODE fitting and trajectory shooting for the first 20 forecast steps, and (3) histogram-tail substitution using synthetic Lorenz libraries for long-time evaluation. A representative mature submission from this system family scored 83.83551 on the public leaderboard, and a small follow-up stack of the same ideas reached 83.85529. We focus on the cleaner intermediate system because it captures the full method while remaining simple enough to reproduce and analyze, while the final submission can be understood as a conservative extension of the same backbone.

### [257] [Training-Free Lexical-Dense Fusion for Conversational-Memory Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04194)
*Christian Lysenstøen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究长对话记忆中的检索瓶颈，通过复现Nano-Memory的工作，探索无需训练、仅在CPU上运行的检索阶段如何提升性能。主要发现包括：（1）将晚期交互密集得分与BM25进行评分级融合，在六个编码器上均显著提升LoCoMo Hit@1达8.8至17.2点，最高达到Hit@1 0.752 / NDCG@5 0.829；（2）使用现成的网页搜索交叉编码器重排序反而导致Hit@1下降6.9个百分点；（3）池化操作中，top-k匹配最大相似度表现最佳，而平滑最大值（log-sum-exp）对一半编码器失效；（4）晚期与早期差距大，且随模型增大而扩大，但融合增益减弱；在词汇主导场景下，融合优势不显著。研究强调了稠密检索与词法检索的分工：稠密方法在多跳和时间类问题上更优，而词法方法在对抗性问题上仍占优。本研究贡献在于提供一个可控、可复现的无训练检索方案，而非完整记忆架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决长对话历史中跨会话查询的检索瓶颈，提升长期对话记忆系统的效率与准确性，尤其关注无需训练、可在低资源环境下运行的检索策略改进。

Method: 复现并扩展Nano-Memory的晚交互检索方法，采用评分级融合（score-level fusion）将密集检索结果与BM25结合，评估不同编码器、池化策略及重排序器的影响，并进行细粒度分类分析以理解各方法的优势场景。

Result: （1）融合方法在六种编码器上显著提升性能，平均提升8.8–17.2点Hit@1，最优达0.752；（2）交叉编码器重排序导致性能下降6.9个百分点；（3）top-k池化优于平滑最大值；（4）稠密方法在多跳与时间类问题中表现更佳，词法方法在对抗性问题中占优；融合在词汇主导任务中增益有限。

Conclusion: 本研究为无训练、纯CPU检索阶段提供了一个可复现且高效的增强方案，强调了稠密与词法检索的互补性，揭示了当前检索技术在不同问题类型下的分工机制，但并未构建完整记忆系统，仅为检索阶段优化。

Abstract: Retrieving the few past turns that answer a new query across long multi-session histories is the retrieval bottleneck behind long-term conversational memory (LoCoMo, LongMemEval). Recent concurrent work, Nano-Memory, shows that scoring a session by the maximum query-turn similarity (late interaction, "Turn Isolation Retrieval") beats mean-pooled session embeddings. We do not claim that effect; we replicate it and ask what a training-free, CPU-only retrieval stage should add around it. We report four findings. (1) Fuse: score-level fusion of the late-interaction dense score with BM25, under a single leave-one-conversation-out weight, adds +8.8 to +17.2 points of LoCoMo Hit@1 over late interaction alone across six encoders (all p<1e-4), reaching Hit@1 0.752 / NDCG@5 0.829 (e5-large-v2), +11.2 pp over BM25. (2) An off-the-shelf web-search cross-encoder reranker over the fused top-10 hurts here, degrading Hit@1 by 6.9 pp (one reranker, one configuration). (3) A pooling-operator ablation shows top-k late interaction matches max-similarity, but a naive smooth-max (log-sum-exp) collapses for half the encoders. (4) The late-minus-early gap is large for all six encoders and tends to be larger for larger ones, while the marginal fusion gain shrinks; on LongMemEval-S, a lexical regime where BM25 saturates, the net fusion gain over BM25 is small and not significant. A per-category analysis frames the gain as a division of labor: dense late interaction helps most on multi-hop and temporal questions but trails BM25 on adversarial ones. The contribution is a controlled, reproducible account of a strong training-free retrieval recipe, not the late-interaction retriever itself (Nano-Memory's). We make no claim to a complete memory architecture; this is a retrieval-stage study.

### [258] [A Geometric View of Counterfactual Behavior: Interaction of Boundary Proximity and Local Support](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04209)
*Ioanna Gemou,Matteo Gamba,Randall Balestriero,Ritambhara Singh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了预训练编码器与线性分类头在生成反事实解释时的行为差异，发现即使预测性能相似，不同模型的反事实可行性与距离也存在显著差异。通过标准化的局部搜索探测，研究揭示决策边界与局部数据支持的交互作用决定了反事实变化是否可行且位于数据支持区域内。改变分类头可显著影响反事实结果而几乎不改变准确率，表明反事实行为是独立于预测性能的一个新维度，对模型选择、鲁棒性和反事实方法可靠性具有重要启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反事实解释方法依赖于输入的小幅语义变化来改变模型预测，但其可行性受模型决策边界与数据分布之间关系的影响。尽管多个模型具有相似的预测性能，其反事实行为却可能截然不同，这提示需要深入理解反事实生成背后的机制，并探索如何系统化改进反事实解释的可靠性与可实现性。

Method: 采用标准化的局部搜索探针，在多个预训练编码器和线性分类头组合上进行实验，固定编码器表示，仅改变分类头，评估反事实解释的可行性、距离及数据支持区域内的可达性，分析决策边界位置与局部数据支持之间的交互作用。

Result: 结果显示，即使在相同表示空间下，仅更换分类头即可显著改变反事实结果，而预测性能保持稳定；反事实是否可行取决于决策边界与局部数据支持的协同作用；利用这一机制可在固定模型中优化反事实搜索效率。

Conclusion: 反事实行为是一个独立于预测性能的重要维度，可通过调整分类头在不牺牲准确率的前提下改变，这对模型选择、系统鲁棒性以及反事实方法的可信度具有深远影响。

Abstract: Counterfactual explanations seek small, semantically meaningful changes to an input that alter a model's prediction, and are widely used to interpret and audit machine learning systems. In modern vision, language, and multimodal systems, pretrained encoders map inputs to representation spaces, and downstream classifier heads impose decision boundaries within those spaces. As a result, the feasibility and distance of nearby counterfactuals depend on boundary placement relative to the data. Yet models with similar predictive performance can differ substantially in whether such changes are achievable and how far representations must move. This work examines this variation using a standardized local search probe across several pretrained encoders and linear classifier heads. Results show that despite similar predictive performance, models differ substantially in their counterfactual behavior. Under fixed representations, varying only the classifier head alters counterfactual outcomes while leaving predictive performance largely unchanged. This variation is explained by the interaction of decision-boundary proximity and local data support, which jointly determine whether prediction changes are both feasible and lie in regions supported by the data, and can also improve counterfactual search within fixed models. Together, these findings identify counterfactual behavior as a distinct dimension beyond predictive performance and show that it can be altered without changing accuracy, with implications for model selection, robustness, and the reliability of counterfactual methods.

### [259] [Edge of Stability Selectively Shapes Learning Across the Data Distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04212)
*Shauna Kwag,Anakha Ganesh,Tomaso Poggio,Pierfrancesco Beneventano*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了边缘稳定性（EoS）不仅是优化过程的全局属性，还具有选择性：它会重新分配学习资源，增强某些数据子集的学习进度，同时抑制其他子集。通过分支干预实验，研究者证实了这一权衡关系，并识别出两个关键条件：1）该子集的平均梯度需与海森矩阵的主特征向量对齐；2）该子集需在训练过程中保持非零梯度幅度。研究通过受控扰动验证了对齐机制的重要性，发现梯度饱和会使分类置信度高的组别被解耦，优势转向输出异常点。结果表明，EoS不仅是一个稳定边界，更是一种调控数据分布中学习分配的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对边缘稳定性的分析将其视为优化过程的全局特性，但未探讨其在不同数据子集间的差异化影响。本研究旨在揭示其选择性行为及其背后的机制，以深化对深度学习优化动态的理解。

Method: 采用分支干预方法，从相同训练状态进入或退出边缘稳定性（EoS）区域，进行因果分析；通过受控扰动改变梯度方向但保持距离，检验梯度对齐的作用；结合交叉熵损失下的梯度饱和现象，分析不同数据组别的学习动态变化。

Result: 发现边缘稳定性具有选择性：仅当数据组的平均梯度与海森矩阵主特征向量对齐且维持非零梯度幅度时，才能从中获益。梯度对齐被破坏后优势消失，而梯度饱和导致高置信度组别被解耦，学习优势转移至输出异常点。

Conclusion: 边缘稳定性不仅是优化过程的稳定边界，更是一种驱动学习在数据分布中选择性分配的关键机制，其效果依赖于梯度方向与海森结构的对齐性以及梯度持续性。

Abstract: Existing analyses of the edge of stability (EoS) treat it as a global property of optimization. We show that it is also selective: the stability constraint redistributes learning across subsets of the training distribution, amplifying progress on some groups while suppressing progress on others. Using a branching intervention that enters or exits the EoS regime from the same training state, we causally demonstrate this trade-off and identify two necessary conditions for a group to benefit. First, its aggregate gradient must align with the top Hessian eigenvector. We isolate this mechanism with a controlled perturbation that preserves distance but randomizes direction, destroying alignment and eliminating the advantage. Second, the group must sustain non-vanishing gradient magnitude over time. Under cross-entropy loss, gradient saturation decouples confidently classified groups, shifting the advantage to output-outliers, whose gradients persist. Together, these results show that EoS functions not only as a stability boundary, but as a mechanism governing the allocation of learning across the data distribution.

### [260] [Recover-LoRA for Aggressive Quantization: Reclaiming Accuracy in 2-Bit Language Models via Low-Rank Adaptation with Knowledge Distillation on Synthetic Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04238)
*Devleena Das,Rajeev Patwari,Elliott Delaye,Ashish Sirasao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对大语言模型（LLM）超低比特量化（2位）的混合精度策略与数据无关的精度恢复方法。通过仅对MLP中的gate和up投影层进行2位量化（W2），其余层保持更高精度（如W4），实现7.5–23.3%的每秒吞吐量（TPS）提升，同时将量化误差限制在可预测的层中。进一步结合Recover-LoRA技术，利用合成数据进行对数蒸馏训练低秩适配器，有效恢复因2位量化损失的精度，在Qwen3-4B上实现了9个基准测试中80–95%的精度恢复，仅需1万条合成样本且无需标注数据。该方法在不同分布外任务上也表现出良好泛化能力，为边缘设备部署提供了高效的后量化精度恢复方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超低比特量化（如2位）虽能显著提升大语言模型推理的吞吐量和内存效率，但通常导致严重精度下降。现有方法难以在极端压缩下维持可用性能，尤其在资源受限的边缘设备部署场景中，亟需一种高效、轻量且无需真实标注数据的精度恢复机制。

Method: 提出选择性混合精度策略（W4/W2-GateUp），仅对MLP中的gate和up投影层进行2位量化；结合Recover-LoRA方法，通过合成数据进行对数蒸馏，训练低秩适配器以恢复被量化层的精度。该方法无需真实标注数据，适用于数据受限或隐私敏感场景。

Result: 在三个模型家族（4B–20B）和两个硬件平台上验证，W4/W2-GateUp配置相比均匀W4量化提升7.5–23.3%的每秒吞吐量（TPS）。在Qwen3-4B上，Recover-LoRA在9/12基准测试中实现80–95%的精度恢复，仅用1万条合成数据即可达到接近甚至媲美使用标注数据的效果，且在分布外任务上具备良好泛化能力。

Conclusion: Recover-LoRA是一种实用、高效的后量化精度恢复工具，能够支持大语言模型在边缘设备上的极致权重压缩，兼顾性能与精度，特别适合数据受限环境下的部署需求。

Abstract: Aggressive weight quantization to 2-bit precision offers substantial throughput and memory gains for large language model (LLM) inference, but typically incurs severe accuracy degradation. These gains are particularly relevant for edge and on-device deployment, where memory capacity and bandwidth are primary constraints. In this work, we extend Recover-LoRA -- a lightweight, data-free accuracy recovery method originally developed for general model weight corruption -- to the setting of ultra-low-bit quantization. We propose a selective mixed-precision strategy in which only gate and up projection layers of the MLP are quantized to 2-bit (W2), while all other linear layers remain at higher precision, yielding a mixed-precision GateUp configuration. We demonstrate via roofline analysis across three model families (4B--20B) and two hardware platforms that a W4/W2-GateUp deployment (4-bit base with 2-bit gate/up) delivers 7.5--23.3\% TPS improvement over uniform W4 depending on model and context length, while confining quantization error to a predictable subset of layers. We then apply Recover-LoRA -- training low-rank adapters on the quantized layers via logit distillation with synthetic data -- to recover accuracy lost from 2-bit quantization of the gate and up layers. In a case study on Qwen3-4B, Recover-LoRA achieves 80--95\% accuracy recovery on 9 of 12 benchmarks, using only 10k synthetic training samples and no labeled data. We further demonstrate that synthetic data performs comparably to curated labeled data for distillation-based recovery, and that recovery generalizes to out-of-distribution evaluation tasks. Our results present Recover-LoRA as a practical post-quantization accuracy recovery tool for aggressive weight compression in deployment settings.

### [261] [RL Excursions during Pre-Training: Re-examining Policy Optimization for LLM training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04272)
*Rachit Bansal,Clara Mohri,Tian Qin,David Alvarez-Melis,Sham Kakade*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究挑战了标准LLM训练流程中仅在预训练和监督微调（SFT）后应用强化学习（RL）的惯例，发现早期应用RL即可有效提升模型性能，甚至在复杂任务上表现优于完整的SFT→RL流程。研究表明，针对性的预训练数据设计比模型规模更能提升RL效果；而RL直接应用于基础检查点可扩展模型分布，但不会损害通用能力，而SFT反而会削弱。通过并行平均融合RL与SFT目标，新方法在各项指标上均优于其他训练方式，并保持模型通用性。整体表明，应更广泛地使用强化学习进行大模型训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型训练通常在预训练和监督微调（SFT）之后才引入强化学习（RL），但这种顺序是否最优尚不明确。本文旨在探索是否可以在更早阶段应用RL，以及其对模型性能、通用能力和分布特性的影响，从而重新思考训练流程的设计。

Method: 从零开始训练大模型，在不同预训练检查点处直接应用强化学习（RL）、监督微调（SFT）及两者组合（如先SFT再RL或并行融合）。通过对比实验评估不同训练路径在复杂任务上的表现，分析模型能力变化，并考察预训练数据组成对RL效果的影响。

Result: 1. 强化学习在早期阶段即有效，常能快速达到完整SFT→RL流程的性能水平；2. 针对性的预训练数据设计显著提升RL效果，甚至超过模型规模的影响；3. 直接在基础检查点上应用RL可扩展模型分布，而“锐化”效应仅出现在RL位于SFT之后时；4. SFT会削弱模型通用能力，而RL则基本保持不变；5. 并行平均融合RL与SFT目标的方法在所有指标上均优于其他训练方式，且维持模型通用性。

Conclusion: 强化学习不应局限于训练流程的后期阶段，而是可以更早介入，甚至作为核心训练机制。通过优化预训练数据和融合RL与SFT目标，可显著提升模型性能与稳定性。这为大模型训练提供了一种更具潜力的新范式。

Abstract: The standard LLM training pipeline applies reinforcement learning (RL) only after pre-training and supervised fine-tuning (SFT). We question this status quo by training a LLM from scratch and applying RL, SFT, and SFT followed by RL directly to intermediate pre-training checkpoints. We find that RL is effective very early, and often matches the full SFT$\to$RL pipeline early as well. Through experiments on harder problems, we find that targeted pre-training data composition is a strong lever for RL effectiveness, even more so than model scale. Beyond reasoning accuracy, applying RL directly to base checkpoints expands the model's distribution; the sharpening effect reported in recent work arises only when RL follows SFT. The general capabilities of the model remain essentially unchanged by RL, while they degrade following SFT. Finally, we merge RL and SFT objectives by parallel averaging, which outperforms across all other training methods discussed, across metrics, while preserving general capabilities. Together, these results suggest that LLM training might benefit from an expanded use of RL.

### [262] [From Ticks to Flows: Dynamics of Neural Reinforcement Learning in Continuous Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04275)
*Saket Tiwari,Tejas Kotwal,George Konidaris*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的理论框架，将连续环境中的深度强化学习建模为连续时间随机过程，结合随机控制思想。通过引入包含探索和随机转移的演员-评论家算法模型，研究了在无限宽度双层神经网络下的两时间尺度动态：环境时间与梯度时间。利用随机微分方程理论，首次推导出在极小学习率下每个梯度步中状态分布的无穷小变化方程。该工作提供了研究过参数化神经网络演员-评论家算法的非参数化方法，并通过一个简单的连续控制任务进行了实证验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度强化学习理论在连续环境中缺乏对过参数化神经网络动态行为的深入理解，尤其在探索与随机转移的建模方面存在不足。因此，亟需一种能够刻画状态演化与学习过程之间关系的理论框架。

Method: 基于随机控制理论，将连续强化学习问题建模为连续时间随机过程；引入两时间尺度分析（环境时间与梯度时间），在无限宽度双层网络假设下，运用随机微分方程推导状态分布的演化方程。

Result: 首次在连续强化学习中推导出状态分布随梯度步演化的微分方程，在极小学习率下成立；理论结果在简单连续控制任务上得到实验验证。

Conclusion: 本工作建立了一个新颖的非参数化理论框架，为理解过参数化神经网络在连续强化学习中的动态行为提供了数学基础，并为未来设计更高效、稳定的算法提供了理论支持。

Abstract: We present a novel theoretical framework for deep reinforcement learning (RL) in continuous environments by modeling the problem as a continuous-time stochastic process, drawing on insights from stochastic control. Building on previous work, we introduce a viable model of actor-critic algorithm that incorporates both exploration and stochastic transitions. For single-hidden-layer neural networks, we show that the state of the environment can be formulated as a two time scale process: the environment time and the gradient time. Within this formulation, we characterize how the time-dependent random variables that represent the environment's state and estimate of the cumulative discounted return evolve over gradient steps in the infinite width limit of two-layer networks. Using the theory of stochastic differential equations, we derive, for the first time in continuous RL, an equation describing the infinitesimal change in the state distribution at each gradient step, under a vanishingly small learning rate. Overall, our work provides a novel nonparametric formulation for studying overparametrized neural actor-critic algorithms. We empirically corroborate our theoretical result using a toy continuous control task.

</details>


### [263] [Derivative Informed Learning of Exchange-Correlation Functionals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04279)
*Eike S. Eberhard,Luca A. Thiede,Abdul Aldossary,Andreas Burger,Nicholas Gao,Vignesh Bhethanabotla,Alán Aspuru-Guzik,Stephan Günnemann*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种名为DI-Loss的新型损失函数，用于训练机器学习交换-关联（XC）泛函，使其在$\mathcal{O}(N^3)$-scaling下模仿B3LYP/def2-SVP混合泛函的表现。DI-Loss通过监督能量在密度矩阵格拉斯曼流形上的第一和第二阶导数，不仅匹配自洽固定点，还对局部响应进行对齐，从而显著提升能量预测精度。在四种不同架构中，总能量平均绝对误差（MAE）相比仅使用能量和密度监督下降66%；密度敏感的均场能量指标$E_ρ$从1.2降至0.8 mEh。此外，衍生泛函可减少混合泛函自洽迭代最多50%，并在下游时间依赖密度泛函理论（TDDFT）计算中改善激发态预测，使激发能平均绝对误差降低19%-35%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统机器学习XC泛函虽能学习参考数据，但尚未一致超越$\mathcal{O}(N^4)$-scaling的混合泛函。本研究旨在通过引入更丰富的物理信息（如梯度与曲率），提升低标度ML-XC泛函的准确性与效率，以实现对高精度混合泛函的有效替代。

Method: 采用混合蒸馏框架，训练$\mathcal{O}(N^3)$-scaling的机器学习XC泛函，使其模仿B3LYP/def2-SVP的结果。提出Derivative Informed XC-Loss（DI-Loss），通过在格拉斯曼流形上监督能量的一阶与二阶导数，增强对泛函局部响应的建模能力。实验评估了四种不同网络架构，并对比了不同监督策略下的性能表现。

Result: DI-Loss在所有架构中均显著提升主能量指标：总能量MAE平均下降66%；$E_ρ$从1.2降至0.8 mEh。密度误差和偶极矩误差未普遍改善。蒸馏后的泛函可将混合泛函的自洽迭代减少高达50%。在TDDFT中，加入赫斯曼监督后，激发能预测误差降低19%-35%。

Conclusion: 通过引入基于导数的监督机制（DI-Loss），机器学习XC泛函能够更准确地模拟高精度混合泛函的局部响应特性，在保持较低计算成本的同时显著提升能量预测精度与自洽收敛速度，并有效改进激发态性质的计算结果，为未来高效、高精度泛函开发提供了新路径。

Abstract: Machine-learned (ML) exchange-correlation (XC) functionals aim to replace human-designed density functional approximations by learning directly from reference data, but they still do not consistently outperform traditional $\mathcal{O}(N^4)$-scaling hybrid functionals. We study a hybrid-distillation setting in which $\mathcal{O}(N^3)$-scaling ML-XC functionals are trained to reproduce B3LYP/def2-SVP targets. We introduce Derivative Informed XC-Loss (DI-Loss), a loss that incorporates additional information from the reference hybrid functional by supervising first and second derivatives of the energy on the Grassmannian of admissible density matrices. Rather than only matching the self-consistent fixed point, DI-Loss aligns the local first- and second-order response of the learned functional with that of the target functional. Across four evaluated architectures, DI-Loss consistently improves the main energy metrics. Averaged uniformly across architectures, the total-energy MAE decreases by 66% relative to energy and density supervision alone. The density-sensitive mean-field energy metric $E_ρ$ improves from $1.2$ to $0.8$ mEh on average, while dipole and $\mathcal{L}_2$ density errors do not improve uniformly. We further show that densities from the distilled functionals reduce hybrid-functional SCF iterations by up to 50%. In downstream TDDFT calculations, Hessian supervision improves excited-state predictions, with XCdiff reducing the mean excitation-energy MAE by 19 - 35%.

### [264] [The Loss Is Not Enough: Sampling Conditions and Inductive Bias in Contrastive Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04280)
*Justinas Zaliaduonis,Patrick Putzky,Till Richter,Sergios Gatidis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种测度论框架，形式化了对比学习中恢复有意义潜在几何结构所需的多样性条件。研究表明，在标准的全支撑冯·米塞斯-费舍尔设置下，该条件成立，全局对比损失最小化器可恢复潜在几何结构（至正交变换）。而受限条件分布可能导致非正交映射达到更低的渐近对比损失。为此，作者引入支持修正的信息噪声对比估计（InfoNCE）变体，理论上可实现正交恢复，但不唯一。合成基准实验验证了可识别性预测，CIFAR-10实验支持当采样多样性受限时，网络架构归纳偏置的重要性上升。整体揭示了采样机制与编码器归纳偏置在对比表示学习中的交互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解对比学习在何种条件下能恢复有意义的潜在几何结构，特别是正则化采样机制对表示质量的影响，是当前自监督学习中的核心问题。现有理论尚不完善，尤其缺乏对正样本采样策略如何影响潜在空间结构的系统分析。

Method: 构建测度论框架，形式化多样性条件；分析不同采样分布（全支撑与受限条件）下的对比损失行为；提出支持修正的InfoNCE变体以修复理论缺陷；通过合成数据与真实图像数据集进行实验验证理论预测。

Result: 在全支撑条件下，对比学习能恢复潜在几何结构至正交变换；受限采样会导致非正交映射更优；支持修正的InfoNCE可实现正交恢复，但不唯一；实验表明采样多样性不足时，模型架构的归纳偏置变得更为关键。

Conclusion: 对比学习的性能高度依赖于采样机制与编码器的归纳偏置之间的协同作用。多样性条件是恢复正确潜在几何的关键，其满足程度决定了是否能实现正交等距映射。支持修正的算法提供了理论保障，但实际选择仍受模型结构影响，提示未来方法需同时优化采样与架构设计。

Abstract: Contrastive learning has become a leading paradigm for self-supervised representation learning, yet the conditions under which it recovers meaningful latent geometry remain incompletely understood. We develop a measure-theoretic framework formalizing the diversity condition, a support requirement on positive-pair sampling that is necessary for isometric latent recovery. We show that the standard full-support von Mises-Fisher setting implies the satisfaction of the diversity condition and as a consequence global contrastive loss minimizers recover latent geometry up to orthogonal transformation, while restricted conditionals can make non-orthogonal maps attain strictly lower asymptotic contrastive loss. We introduce a support-corrected Information Noise Contrastive Estimation (InfoNCE) variant as a theoretical fix: this correction makes orthogonal latent space recovery achievable but does not uniquely select it. Experiments on synthetic benchmarks validate the identifiability predictions, and CIFAR-10 experiments are consistent with the qualitative prediction that architectural inductive bias becomes more important when sampling diversity is limited. Together, our results clarify how sampling mechanisms and encoder inductive bias interact in contrastive representation learning.

To address this limitation without additional annotation costs, recent work has proposed learning multiple preference components from binary data and combining them to model individual preferences. Method: 采用结构引导的拓扑排序将图序列化为边序列，实现高效生成；使用两阶段训练策略，第一阶段进行探索性数据增强，第二阶段进行迭代细化以减少过拟合并引入可控新颖性；支持LSTM与Mamba类因果序列模型，利用大内存加速器处理长序列图生成任务。

In addition, these models often imitate training graphs rather than generalize beyond them.
  We propose a lightweight autoregressive framework to address these issues. It uses a structure-guided topological ordering to serialize graphs into regular edge sequences, enabling near log-linear generation, and a two-phase training strategy that combines exploration-oriented augmentation with iterative refinement to reduce overfitting and promote controlled novelty.

### [267] [PE-MHL: Physics-Encoded Modular Hybrid Layers for Scalable Learning of Complex Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04290)
*Ismail Hassaballa,Mircea Lazar*

Method: 提出物理编码模块化混合层（PE-MHL）框架，采用增量式建模策略：以物理基线模型为基础，逐次引入新的子模型，每个子模型通过最小二乘法初始化，确保整体训练误差不增加，并实现渐进式学习与复杂度控制。

Abstract: Hybrid models that combine physics-based and data-driven components have shown strong potential for achieving accuracy and interpretability in control applications. While recent methods have made progress in incorporating physical consistency, challenges remain in scalability, robustness to noise, and control of model complexity. This paper proposes a Physics-Encoded Modular Hybrid Layer (PE-MHL) framework, in which a baseline physics-based model is incrementally refined through the addition of new sub-models, where each new component adds complexity while preserving what previous components have already learned. We establish a theoretical guarantee for this construction: with a least-squares initialization of each new sub-model, the training error is monotonically non-increasing in the number of sub-models and provably converges. Empirical evaluations on a nonlinear NARX benchmark and the Quanser Aero 2 platform demonstrate that PE-MHL outperforms equivalently sized monolithic networks in both accuracy and generalization, while also providing more stable training dynamics and better preservation of underlying data structures.

Abstract: We study online learning with an additional offline dataset in the stochastic linear bandit setting. Although this problem arises frequently in practice, the offline-to-online tradeoff remains poorly understood in structured environments. We propose a linear bandit algorithm that balances this tradeoff: it relies on offline data during early rounds, and increasingly favors exploration as the horizon grows. We establish regret bounds showing that our method is simultaneously competitive with both purely online and purely offline solutions. In particular, it achieves sublinear regret relative to the optimal action in the number of online interactions, while its regret relative to an offline reference decreases as the number of offline samples grows. Empirical results further demonstrate its effectiveness across various problem parameters.

### [269] [Folded Transport MCMC: Certifiable Quotient Posterior Computation for Symmetric Bayesian Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04307)
*Jun Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Folded Transport MCMC (FolT-MCMC)，通过在对称群的基本域上构建独立采样器，直接对商后验进行推断，解决标签置换对称性导致的冗余多模态问题。利用对称化的归一化流构造商提议分布，并证明其在稳定子修正的球质量界和改进覆盖半径下，保持LCNF振荡认证框架的有效性。实验显示，在高维高斯混合、标签交换目标及真实加速度计数据中，认证改进比达2倍至145倍，折叠证书几乎与维度无关，且在真实数据中实现非空认证而传统方法为真空认证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统MCMC在具有有限对称性的贝叶斯模型（如可交换分量混合模型、紧密邻近模式的结构识别）中，因标签置换对称性导致后验多重模态冗余，严重降低收敛诊断效果。现有方法难以有效处理此类对称性带来的计算挑战，亟需一种能直接在商空间上高效推断的新方法。

Method: 提出Folded Transport MCMC（FolT-MCMC），基于对称群的基本域构建独立采样器；使用学习的归一化流对群轨道进行对称化以生成商提议分布；引入稳定子修正的球质量边界与改进的覆盖半径，将LCNF振荡认证框架推广至商度量空间。

Result: 在二维到二十维的高斯混合模型、最多24个等价模态的标签交换目标以及标准三组分贝叶斯混合后验中，量化核心认证改进比达到2倍至145倍；折叠认证结果在实践中几乎不随维度增长；在台风期间超高层建筑加速度计真实数据中，实现了非空认证，而原始未折叠方法为真空认证。

Conclusion: FolT-MCMC有效解决了由对称性引起的冗余多模态问题，显著提升MCMC收敛诊断能力，在高维和真实场景下表现出卓越性能，为对称性贝叶斯模型提供了更可靠、高效的推断框架。

Abstract: Bayesian models with finite symmetry - mixture models with exchangeable components, structural identification with closely-spaced modes - define posteriors that are invariant under a group of label permutations, creating redundant multimodality that degrades MCMC convergence diagnostics. We introduce Folded Transport MCMC (FolT-MCMC), which performs inference directly on the quotient posterior by constructing an independence sampler on the fundamental domain of the symmetry group. The quotient proposal is formed by symmetrising a learned normalising flow over the group orbits. We prove that the LCNF oscillation-based certification framework transfers to the quotient metric with a stabiliser-corrected ball-mass bound and improved covering radius, and that the quantile-core certified lower bound improves whenever the unfolded flow exhibits cross-mode proposal deficiency. On Gaussian mixtures (d = 2 - 20), label-switching targets (up to 24 equivalent modes), and a standard Bayesian three-component mixture posterior, the quantile-core certified improvement ratio ranges from 2x to 145x, with the folded certificate empirically nearly dimension-free. On real accelerometer data from a supertall building during Typhoon Mangkhut, FolT-MCMC yields a non-vacuous quantile-core certificate where the unfolded certificate is vacuous.

</details>


### [270] [Latent Anchor-Driven Test Generation for Deep Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04310)
*Bin Duan,Matthew B. Dwyer,Guowei Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Latte是一种基于潜在空间的黑盒测试框架，通过预训练的VQ-VAE编码输入种子，在潜在空间中沿来自其他类别的锚点方向进行单步突变，再经量化和解码回输入空间，生成语义相近、多样且能揭示缺陷的测试用例。该方法在保持低语义漂移的同时，提升了故障暴露率和行为多样性，适用于多种数据集和模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有DNN测试方法在输入空间或潜在空间探索中面临探索可控性、故障多样性与种子相关语义漂移之间的权衡，亟需一种更高效、更鲁棒的测试框架。

Method: 使用预训练VQ-VAE编码输入种子，基于其他类别锚点定义突变方向，进行种子中心的一步潜在空间突变，结合量化与解码生成新样本，以探索潜在流形上的局部邻域。

Result: 在5个数据集和10个DNN模型上评估显示，Latte在相同测试预算下显著提升故障暴露率和行为多样性；在单模型场景中有效控制了种子间的语义漂移。

Conclusion: Latte通过潜在空间的可控且多样化的突变策略，实现了对DNN模型更高效、更全面的测试，为安全敏感应用中的模型验证提供了有力支持。

Abstract: Deep Neural Networks (DNNs) are increasingly being deployed in security-critical and safety-sensitive applications, which makes rigorous testing essential to identify and mitigate model weaknesses. Existing DNN testing approaches explore either the input space or a learned latent space. While latent-space generation can better maintain plausibility than direct input-space mutation, current methods still face a trade-off among exploration controllability, failure diversity, and seed-relative semantic drift. To overcome these limitations, we propose Latte, a black-box testing framework that generates semantically proximate, diverse, and fault-revealing test cases by leveraging the latent space. Specifically, Latte encodes each input seed with a pre-trained VQ-VAE and performs a seed-centered, one-step latent mutation along directions defined by anchors sampled from alternative classes, followed by quantization and decoding back to the input space. This explores local neighborhoods around each seed within the learned latent manifold, resulting in a larger number and broader diversity of oracle-triggering prediction discrepancies under the same budget. We evaluated Latte on 5 datasets and 10 DNN models in single-model and multi-model testing scenarios. Across the evaluated datasets and models, Latte improves fault exposure and behavioral diversity under matched testing budgets. Under the single-model setting, it also maintains low seed-relative semantic drift with respect to the source seeds.

Method: BayesWarp结合可解释的显著性分析识别决策关键输入区域，并采用不确定性感知的贝叶斯优化策略自适应地指导测试过程，以实现高效且语义合理的输入变异。

Abstract: As neural networks are increasingly deployed in safety-critical domains, testing is essential to evaluate and improve their reliability. Existing testing methods, whether black-box or white-box, primarily use global mutation or coverage-guided strategies, both of which struggle to efficiently uncover diverse model failures while remaining proximate to the original data distribution and semantics. We propose BayesWarp, a testing framework that addresses this limitation by mutating decision-critical input regions identified via interpretable saliency techniques and adaptively guiding the testing process using an uncertainty-aware Bayesian Optimization strategy, enabling the discovery of diverse failures while preserving distributional and semantic proximity to the original data. Evaluation on MNIST, CIFAR-10, and ImageNet across six neural network models shows that BayesWarp improves failure discovery, failure diversity, test case quality, and critical neuron coverage under a fixed mutation budget. These results demonstrate that BayesWarp improves testing effectiveness. Moreover, fine-tuning with the generated failure cases leads to improvements in model performance.
