### [272] [OpenRFM: Dissecting Relational In-Context Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04320)
*Zhikai Chen,Junyu Yin,Jialiang Gu,Siheng Xiong,Xiaoze Liu,Ruowang Zhang,Keren Zhou,Kai Guo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究分析了开放型关系基础模型（RFM）与商业模型之间的性能差距，指出其根源在于关系级上下文学习（ICL）的局限性及预训练数据的不足。通过剖析Relational Transformer（RT）框架，发现其在稀疏标签覆盖下会因回归欠定而失效，并揭示了标签生成过程中缺乏可识别的关系潜在结构这一关键缺失。为此，提出OpenRFM：结合双阶段ICL架构和融合同质性感知的合成+持续真实数据混合预训练策略，显著提升性能，平均任务表现提升约30%，超越商业模型KumoRFMv1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开放型关系基础模型（RFM）在性能上远落后于商业模型，但其根本原因尚未被系统理解，亟需深入分析模型与数据两方面的瓶颈，以推动开放生态的发展。

Method: 从模型与数据双视角剖析典型框架Relational Transformer（RT），揭示其关系级ICL的局限性；提出双阶段ICL架构与同质性感知的合成+持续真实数据混合预训练方案，引入原型正则化增强泛化能力。

Result: 所提出的OpenRFM在多个评估任务上实现平均性能提升约30%，并超越商业模型KumoRFMv1，验证了方法的有效性与实用性。

Conclusion: 性能差距源于模型层面的关系级标签稀缺与数据层面的预训练不充分；通过设计支持批量级ICL与增强泛化能力的预训练策略，OpenRFM有效弥合了开放与商业模型间的鸿沟。

Abstract: Relational Foundation Models (RFMs) promise a single pre-trained predictor that, given any relational database, returns predictions in one forward pass via relational in-context learning (ICL). Yet a substantial gap separates open RFMs from their commercial counterparts, and the origin of this gap has not been systematically understood. We dissect a representative framework, the Relational Transformer (RT), from two perspectives. Model side: we show that RT performs relation-level ICL, and a kernel regression view shows it fails when sparse label-cell coverage yields an underdetermined regression. Data side: we ablate RT's pre-training source and find that existing synthetic-only pre-training and in-distribution pre-training drive the same architecture into different regimes, lazy vs. feature-learning. Probing this gap reveals that the missing ingredient is a support-identifiable relational latent in the label-generation process. These two diagnoses translate into (1) a dual-stage ICL architecture that combines the relational backbone with a batch-level ICL layer lifted from a pre-trained tabular foundation model to overcome relation-level label scarcity, and (2) a homophily-aware synthetic plus continual real-data pre-training mixture, augmented with a prototype-based regularization. These choices define OpenRFM, a simple yet effective RFM that improves average task performance by approximately 30% over the RT backbone and surpasses the commercial model KumoRFMv1 on a large set of evaluation tasks.

### [273] [Neural Galerkin Normalizing Flows for Bayesian Inference of Diffusions with Inaccessible Boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04324)
*Riccardo Saporiti,Fabio Nobile*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的归一化流架构，通过神经伽辽金框架求解以狄拉克质量为初始条件的福克-普朗克方程，学习扩散过程在相邻观测时间之间的转移密度函数。该方法特别适用于扩散矩阵在某些不可达边界区域消失的模型（如满足费勒条件的随机波动率模型）。训练后可高效近似似然函数，实现快速贝叶斯推断，避免实时求解福克-普朗克方程或依赖模拟桥接的无似然方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于离散观测下扩散模型的转移密度函数缺乏解析表达式，导致贝叶斯推断难以进行。现有方法或需反复模拟扩散桥，或依赖近似似然，效率低且精度受限。因此亟需一种高效、准确的学习转移密度的方法。

Method: 采用归一化流结合神经伽辽金框架，求解福克-普朗克方程，初始条件为狄拉克质量，训练分布覆盖初始状态与扩散系数的多样性。通过学习转移密度，构建可观测轨迹上的似然近似。

Result: 所提方法在训练完成后可高效生成转移密度估计，显著提升贝叶斯推断效率；在真实数据和合成数据上均表现出良好性能，支持低成本的马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛采样。

Conclusion: 该方法成功将复杂扩散模型的似然计算问题转化为可训练的神经网络学习任务，为高维、非线性扩散模型提供了高效的贝叶斯推断新范式。

Abstract: One of the primary challenges in Bayesian inference on the parameters of a diffusion model from discrete observations is the unavailability of an analytical expression for the transition density function between consecutive observation times, which is needed to derive the likelihood function.
  Extending previous studies that solve Fokker-Planck (FP) type partial differential equations with Normalizing Flows, we propose a new Normalizing Flow architecture to learn the transition density function of the diffusion process between two observation times. We do so by solving in a Neural Galerkin framework the associated FP equation with a Dirac mass as initial condition, over a specified training distribution of the initial datum and the coefficients of the diffusion. We specifically focus on processes whose diffusion matrix vanishes in certain inaccessible boundary regions, such as Stochastic Volatility models that satisfy a Feller condition.
  The product of the obtained transition densities evaluated along the observed trajectory approximates the likelihood function, thereby enabling cheap posterior sampling via Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC). After the offline training phase, inference becomes significantly more efficient, as it avoids the need to solve the FP equation in real time for each parameter proposed by the MCMC sampler or to rely on other likelihood-free methods for Bayesian inference that involve repeated simulation of diffusion bridges.

This limits researchers' ability to determine which problems are suitable for these models, isolate the factors that drive their performance or lead to failures, or uncover which algorithms perform well. ### [275] [A Geometric Characterization of the Stationary Plateau for Two-Layer Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04327)
*Tian Ding,Dawei Li,Ruoyu Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有平滑激活函数的两层神经网络损失景观中出现的静态平台的几何结构，重点分析了‘神经元分裂’现象：将一个隐藏神经元复制后，在更宽的网络中产生一个仿射的驻点集。作者对这些平台上的所有驻点进行了全面分类，确定了在何种条件下它们构成局部极小值或鞍点。分析的核心是一个称为‘内海森矩阵’的每神经元曲率对象。结果表明，内海森矩阵的正定性与分裂系数的选择共同决定了平台的局部几何性质。研究发现，将局部极小值进行分裂可能产生局部极小值和鞍点的混合，或全为鞍点的平台，并在温和假设下识别出确定的鞍点区域；而分裂鞍点则始终产生鞍点平台。该工作统一并扩展了先前的景观分析，阐明了模型扩展如何保持或改变驻点性质，为宽度扩展与重参数化在神经网络中的几何影响提供了新的见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解神经网络损失景观中由于网络宽度增加引发的几何变化，特别是‘神经元分裂’现象对驻点性质的影响，以揭示模型扩展如何保留或改变优化过程中的局部极小值结构。

Method: 通过构建并分析‘内海森矩阵’这一每神经元曲率对象，结合分裂系数的选取，对两层神经网络中由神经元分裂产生的静态平台上的驻点进行分类，利用矩阵正定性与分裂策略联合判断其是否为局部极小值或鞍点。

Result: 分裂局部极小值可能导致混合极小值与鞍点，或形成全鞍点平台；分裂鞍点则必然生成全鞍点平台；在温和假设下可明确界定鞍点区域。研究揭示了宽度扩展对驻点性质的决定性影响。

Conclusion: 本研究通过引入内海森矩阵，系统刻画了神经元分裂导致的平台几何结构，揭示了宽度扩展如何改变优化景观的局部性质，为理解神经网络重参数化与宽度扩展的几何效应提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We investigate the geometric structure of stationary plateaus that arise in the loss landscape of two-layer neural networks with smooth activation functions. We focus on the phenomenon of "neuron splitting" where duplicating a hidden neuron yields an affine set of stationary points in a wider network. We provide a comprehensive classification of all stationary points on these plateaus, determining under what conditions they constitute local minima or saddle points. Our characterization hinges on a per-neuron curvature object we term the "inner Hessian" matrix. Our analysis reveals that the definiteness of the inner Hessian and the choice of splitting coefficients jointly dictate the local geometry of the plateau. We show that "splitting" a local minimum can yield either a mixture of local minima and saddles or an all-saddle plateau, with a concrete sure-saddle region identified under mild assumptions. In contrast, splitting a saddle point always produces a plateau of saddle points. Our results unify and extend prior landscape analyses, elucidating when and how model expansion preserves or alters the nature of stationary points. These findings offer new geometric insights into the effects of width expansion and reparameterization in neural networks.

### [276] [Policy Gradient for Continuous-Time Robust Markov Decision Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04335)
*Tanya Veeravalli,David M. Bossens,Atsushi Nitanda*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究连续时间鲁棒马尔可夫决策过程（RMDP）中的策略梯度算法，推导了基于路径和伴随公式的随机与常微分方程的策略梯度和对抗梯度。提出双循环优化器实现原问题设定下的线性收敛及样本设定下$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{1}{ε^2})$的样本复杂度，并引入均值场优化器实现分布优化，具有$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{1}{K})$的原问题收敛率和$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{N^2}{ε})$的样本复杂度。实验验证了在神经常微分方程动态下的连续时间策略梯度算法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统鲁棒马尔可夫决策过程（RMDP）主要针对离散时间动态，而现实中许多系统是连续时间的。现有方法在连续时间框架下的样本效率和理论保证仍不充分，因此需要发展适用于连续时间动态的高效、稳健的策略梯度算法。

Method: 采用路径和伴随法推导连续时间系统中策略梯度与对抗梯度；设计双循环优化器以实现线性收敛和低样本复杂度；提出均值场优化器用于分布级优化，结合$N$粒子近似分析其收敛性能。

Result: 双循环优化器在原问题设定下实现线性收敛，在样本设定下达到$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{1}{ε^2})$的样本复杂度；均值场优化器在原问题设定下实现$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{1}{K})$的收敛率，样本复杂度为$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{N^2}{ε})$；实验表明在神经常微分方程动态下算法有效。

Conclusion: 本工作首次系统地建立了连续时间鲁棒马尔可夫决策过程中的策略梯度理论框架，提出了高效的双循环与均值场优化算法，显著提升了连续时间系统的样本效率与理论保障，为复杂动态系统的鲁棒强化学习提供了新工具。

Abstract: The framework of robust Markov decision processes (RMDPs) allows the design of reinforcement learning agents that satisfy performance guarantees under worst-case transition dynamics. Traditional RMDPs consider discrete-time dynamics and recently, sample-efficient policy gradient algorithms have been considered in this context. This paper investigates policy gradient algorithms within a continuous-time RMDP framework. Policy gradients and adversarial gradients are derived using pathwise and adjoint-based formulas for stochastic and ordinary differential equations. We propose double-loop optimisers to obtain linear convergence in the oracle-based setting and an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{1}{ε^2})$ sample complexity in the sample-based setting in an analysis which also derives novel tools for the framework of undiscounted total cost MDPs. Additionally, we propose mean-field optimisers as distributional optimisers with an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{1}{K})$ oracle-based convergence rate and an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\frac{N^2}ε)$ sample complexity under $N$-particle approximation. The effectiveness of continuous-time policy gradient algorithms is confirmed for both optimisers on continuous-time RMDPs with neural ordinary differential equation dynamics.

</details>

Abstract: Privacy-sensitive and distributed characteristics of multi-center medical data bring severe obstacles to centralized modeling for accurate early prediction of sepsis. Federated learning (FL) has attracted growing attention as a promising framework for collaborative model development, as it allows multiple institutions to jointly train predictive models without directly sharing or centralizing raw data. Nevertheless, its practical performance, robustness, and privacy-preserving benefits remain insufficiently evaluated using real-world clinical datasets. To bridge this gap, this study systematically examines the application of federated learning to multi-center sepsis prediction. The experimental dataset consists of 648 clinically screened samples collected from three tertiary hospitals in China, with rigorous inclusion and exclusion criteria. Extensive experimental results demonstrate that the federated learning-based model achieves highly comparable prediction accuracy to the centralized counterpart, while fundamentally avoiding privacy leakage. Further privacy security analysis verifies that malicious attackers cannot reconstruct the original patient data from the transmitted model parameters, indicating strong resistance against data reconstruction attacks. This work not only validates the practicality and security of federated learning in clinical sepsis prediction, but also provides a reliable and feasible solution for privacy-preserving multi-center medical collaboration.

### [278] [Literature-Guided Minimax Optimization of Virtual Epilepsy Neurostimulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04339)
*Cathy Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种文献引导的极小化极大（minimax）流程，结合PubMed级假设提取、The Virtual Brain (TVB) Epileptor模拟和大语言模型驱动的黑箱优化，旨在设计对最脆弱患者也有效的神经调控方案。该方法通过最大化最差情况下的奖励（即最小化癫痫活动方差），实现稳健的个性化治疗设计。在内在参数优化中，最优参数集使最差情况奖励提升39.8%；而外部刺激方案虽有55%应答率，但在20名虚拟患者中未见整体改善（p=0.9019），提示个体差异显著。研究为计算驱动的鲁棒神经调控设计提供了概念验证，非临床证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用文献引导的极小化极大框架，结合PubMed级假设提取、TVB Epileptor仿真与大语言模型驱动的黑箱优化。优化器可生成内在控制参数或临床可解释的外部刺激方案；TVB在多个虚拟患者中评估每项提案；目标函数为最大化最差情况下的奖励，即最小化癫痫活动的方差。

Result: 内在模型控制参数优化中，最差情况奖励从-0.5285提升至-0.3182，提升39.8%；外部刺激方案仅带来1.7%最差情况改善，20人虚拟队列无统计学意义的整体提升（p=0.9019），尽管有55%应答率和颞叶亚组正向信号。

Abstract: Computational models of epilepsy promise patient-specific treatment design, but most optimization workflows still search for parameters that perform well on average. In neuromodulation, this is a weak target: a protocol that improves the mean response can still fail in the patient whose network is least tolerant to stimulation. We present a literature-guided minimax pipeline that couples PubMed-scale hypothesis extraction, The Virtual Brain (TVB) Epileptor simulations, and large-language-model-guided black-box optimization. The optimizer proposes either intrinsic model-control parameters or clinically interpretable external-stimulation protocols; TVB evaluates each proposal across sampled virtual patients; and the objective maximizes worst-case reward, defined as the negative variance of simulated seizure activity. In the intrinsic model-control experiment, the best archived parameter set improved worst-case reward from -0.5285 to -0.3182, a 39.8% gain over baseline. The clinical-style external-stimulation search produced a much smaller worst-case improvement (1.7%), and a 20-patient virtual cohort showed no aggregate benefit (p=0.9019), despite a 55% responder rate and a positive temporal-lobe subgroup signal. The study should be read as an in silico proof of concept for robust, literature-aware neurostimulation design, not as clinical evidence.

### [279] [Expectations vs. Realities: The Cost of MSE-Optimal Forecasting Under Conditional Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04342)
*Riku Green,Zahraa S. Abdallah,Telmo M Silva Filho*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究多步时间序列预测（MSF）中仅使用均方误差（MSE）等点误差指标评估模型的局限性，指出在条件不确定性较高时，条件均值无法代表实际观测值，导致MSE最优模型可能严重低估未来分布的变异性。作者提出‘条件不确定性差距’概念，证明无论何种模型，都无法同时最小化MSE并准确匹配真实未来的边际分布，从而揭示了点准确性与边际现实性之间的根本性权衡。通过模拟系统和九个真实世界基准测试，实证发现随着预测范围延长，可实现的解集形成明显的帕累托前沿：轻微放松MSE（≤5%）即可带来显著的边际现实性提升（中位数17.3%，部分达30%以上）。不同预测策略位于该前沿的不同位置：直接多输出模型趋向精度最优但方差不足，而递归方法和基于样本的推断则更注重现实性。因此，本文强调了在长周期预测中应重新审视评价标准，并将模型选择视为在准确性与现实性之间权衡的过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多步时间序列预测普遍依赖均方误差（MSE）等点误差指标，但这些指标在条件不确定性增加时会失效，无法反映真实未来的分布特征，尤其在长期预测中可能导致模型低估变异性，从而产生误导性的评估结果。

Method: 提出条件不确定性差距理论框架，从理论上证明点预测器在存在非零条件不确定性时无法同时最小化MSE并匹配真实边际分布；通过控制的随机动力系统和多个真实世界数据集进行实验验证，构建并刻画准确性-现实性前沿（accuracy-realism frontier），分析不同预测策略在该前沿上的分布特征。

Result: 在长期预测中，条件不确定性导致MSE最优模型往往低估未来波动性，造成严重的边际分布失真；小幅放宽MSE要求（≤5%）即可带来显著的现实性提升（中位17.3%，最高超30%）；不同预测方法（如直接多输出、递归、样本推断）分别占据准确性或现实性优势区域，形成清晰的帕累托前沿。

Conclusion: MSE-only评价体系在长周期多步预测中存在结构性缺陷，无法捕捉模型的现实性表现。模型选择应被视为在准确性与边际现实性之间的权衡过程，未来评价需引入对分布特性的考量，以避免误导性结论。

Abstract: Multi-step time series forecasting (MSF) is commonly evaluated using point-wise error metrics such as mean squared error (MSE), implicitly treating the conditional mean as a sufficient target. We show that this can be misleading under conditional uncertainty, where the conditional expectation becomes unrepresentative of typical realized values at longer horizons. We formalize this effect through a conditional uncertainty gap and prove that whenever this gap is nonzero, no deterministic predictor can simultaneously minimize MSE and match the marginal distribution of realized futures. This establishes a fundamental, model-agnostic trade-off between point accuracy and marginal realism in MSF evaluation. Using controlled stochastic dynamical systems and nine real-world forecasting benchmarks, we empirically characterize the resulting accuracy--realism frontier and \textbf{quantify the practical cost of MSE-only model selection}. As conditional uncertainty increases with forecast horizon, the attainable set expands into a pronounced Pareto front, separating MSE-optimal but under-dispersed predictors from methods that trade accuracy for realistic marginal variability. \textbf{Across benchmarks, we find that small relaxations in MSE ($\boldsymbol{\le 5\%}$) frequently unlock disproportionate gains in marginal realism, with median improvements of $\mathbf{17.3\%}$ and gains exceeding $\mathbf{30\%}$ in some datasets.} We further show that common forecasting strategies systematically occupy different regions of this frontier: direct multi-output predictors concentrate near the accuracy-optimal extreme, while recursive strategies and sample-based inference favors marginal realism. Together, these results expose a structural failure mode of MSE-based evaluation in long-horizon forecasting and recast strategy and inference selection as navigation of an unavoidable accuracy--realism trade-off.

</details>


### [280] [MeshTok: Efficient Multi-Scale Tokenization for Scalable PDE Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04366)
*Yanshun Zhao,Xiaoyu Peng,Jiamin Jiang,Congcong Zhu,Jingrun Chen*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出MeshTok框架，利用自适应网格细化（AMR）思想，对具有显著特征的区域进行空间细化，生成多尺度异构标记，并在统一的Transformer架构中进行处理，实现粗粒度全局与细粒度局部信息的联合建模。

Conclusion: 自适应多尺度标记化可有效提升神经网络对复杂偏微分方程的建模效率，是值得推广的通用设计范式。

Abstract: Conventional patchified Transformers operate on uniform spatial partitions, distributing computational effort evenly across the domain irrespective of local features. This inflexible tokenization scheme is inherently limited in its ability to efficiently represent and process solutions to complex PDEs. To address this, we propose MeshTok, an adaptive mesh refinement (AMR)-inspired tokenization and sequence modeling framework. This method selectively refines spatial regions exhibiting sharp gradients, transient features, or multiscale structures, generating a heterogeneous set of multiscale tokens defined on a fixed simulation grid. These tokens are processed within a unified Transformer sequence, enabling the model to simultaneously capture coarse-grained global context and fine-grained local details without requiring specialized architectural components. Although adaptive refinement moderately increases token count, it promotes a more targeted allocation of computational resources to physically informative regions, which we view as a practical inductive bias rather than a formal optimality guarantee. Experimental evaluations across multiple PDE families and benchmark datasets demonstrate that MeshTok consistently improves the efficiency-accuracy trade-off compared to uniform-grid baselines. This suggests adaptive multiscale tokenization as a scalable and generalizable design principle for neural PDE modeling. Code is available at https://github.com/SCAILab-USTC/MeshTok.

### [281] [When Do Fewer Coordinates Suffice in DP-SGD?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04375)
*Huiqi Zhang,Fang Xie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出TP-TopK方法，通过两阶段机制在不依赖公开数据的情况下实现坐标稀疏的差分隐私训练。第一阶段私有预热识别关键坐标支持集，第二阶段基于该支持集进行高效训练。理论分析表明，在特定条件下噪声规模由活跃维度k决定而非全维度d，实验验证了学习到的坐标支持比随机选择更有效，尤其在活跃维度小且预热评分可靠时收益显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统DP-SGD在高维参数空间中注入与维度d成比例的噪声，导致隐私成本过高；本文旨在减少更新坐标数量以降低噪声影响，同时保持优化信号。

Method: 提出两阶段方法TP-TopK：第一阶段使用私有方式收集梯度信息并识别重要坐标（支持集）；第二阶段仅在这些坐标上进行梯度更新，从而降低噪声能量。理论分析结合非凸优化站位性边界，证明在满足条件时噪声缩放为活跃维度k。

Result: 实验在MNIST、FMNIST和CIFAR-10上显示，学习得到的坐标支持能保留更多梯度能量，优于同尺寸随机支持；当活跃维度小且预热评分准确时性能提升最明显。

Conclusion: TP-TopK通过坐标稀疏化有效降低了差分隐私训练中的噪声负担，实现了在低维子空间内高效优化，为高维模型的隐私训练提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Differentially private stochastic gradient descent (DP-SGD) injects noise into every updated coordinate, making the injected noise energy scale with the ambient parameter dimension \(d\). We ask when private training can update fewer coordinates without losing the signal needed for optimization. We propose \textsc{TP-TopK} (Two-Phase TopK DP-SGD), a two-phase method for coordinate-sparse private training without public data, in which a private warm-up phase identifies a coordinate support used to guide the main training phase. We give a criterion characterizing when coordinate restriction can be beneficial, show via a nonconvex stationarity bound that under this condition the relevant noise term scales with the active dimension \(k\) rather than the full parameter dimension \(d\), and provide a lower bound on the reliability of warm-up-based coordinate ranking. Experiments on MNIST, FMNIST, and CIFAR-10 show that learned coordinate supports can retain more gradient energy than size-matched random supports, with the largest gains when the active dimension is small and warm-up scores are informative.

### [282] [From Symbolic to Geometric: Enabling Spatial Reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04381)
*Chen Chu,Bita Azarijoo,Li Xiong,Khurram Shafique,Cyrus Shahabi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型的空间推理能力主要依赖于对空间语言模式的匹配，属于符号化推理，缺乏对连续空间表示、显式几何计算和结构化空间操作的支持。因此需要一种能真正进行几何空间推理的新模型。

Method: 提出Spatial Language Model (SLM)，将位置信息作为第一类模态，直接在学习到的空间表征上进行推理；构建Spatial Instruction Dataset以对齐空间表示、几何操作与自然语言指令；设计SpatialEval基准用于评估多维度空间推理能力。

Abstract: Recent large language models (LLMs) often appear to exhibit spatial reasoning ability; however, this capability is largely \emph{symbolic}, arising from pattern matching over spatial language rather than true \emph{geometric} reasoning over space. Because LLMs operate on discrete tokens, they lack native support for continuous spatial representations, explicit geometric computation, and structured spatial operators. To address this limitation, we introduce the \emph{Spatial Language Model (SLM)}, the first multimodal LLM that treats location information as a first-class modality and enables geometric spatial reasoning within the model's inference process. SLM directly operates on learned spatial representations rather than textual descriptions of spatial relations. To support effective training, we construct a \emph{Spatial Instruction Dataset} that aligns spatial representations, atomic geometric operations, and natural language instructions. We further propose a new benchmark named \emph{SpatialEval}, which is designed to evaluate spatial reasoning across attributes, distance, topology, and relative-position tasks. Extensive experiments show that SLM significantly outperforms existing LLM-based approaches that rely on symbolic reasoning via prompt engineering or textual abstraction, demonstrating the benefits of integrating geometric spatial representations for robust spatial reasoning.
  Our instruction dataset, evaluation benchmark, model training codes, and models' checkpoints can be found at:
  \hyperlink{https://github.com/chuchen2017/SLM}{https://github.com/chuchen2017/SLM}.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Gardner体积比较和哈里什-钱德拉-伊茨科恩-祖伯（HCIZ）公式，结合Weyl积分公式与Haar测度，对酉和正交紧凑流形进行积分分析。

Result: 得到了实预激活与复数预激活在相同假设类中存储容量的渐近比例，并获得了更鲁棒的近似结果。

Conclusion: HCIZ公式在临界容量下的应用为复杂假设类中的存储容量分析提供了新方法，显著提升了渐近比估计的精度。

Abstract: We find the asymptotic ratio between the storage capacities when enforcing real pre-activations in a complex hypothesis class as opposed to complex ones in the same class. Our methods depend on Gardner volume comparisons at critical capacity. Our proof relies on an application of the Harish-Chandra-Itzykson-Zuber (HCIZ) formula, nonstandard in literature. With the HCIZ formula, we may obtain a more robust approximation for the final asymptotic ratio. This strategy is applicable to our work specifically since we integrate over the unitary and orthogonal compact manifolds, facilitated via the Weyl integration formula and the Haar measure.

### [285] [Physics-Informed Neural Network Modeling of Biodegradable Contaminant Transport through GCL/SL Composite Liners](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04392)
*Dong Li,Yapeng Cao,Haiping Zhao,Shutong Han*

Abstract: This study develops a two-domain physics-informed neural network framework for contaminant transport through a GCL/SL composite liner system, in which the thin GCL layer is treated using a steady-state advection-dispersion-biodegradation formulation and the underlying soil liner is modeled as a transient transport domain. Two formulations are evaluated against analytical and finite-element reference solutions under different leachate-head conditions: a standard PINN with soft constraint enforcement (Std-PINN) and a hard-constrained PINN (H-PINN), in which selected boundary and initial conditions are embedded directly into the trial solutions. The Std-PINN captures the overall breakthrough behavior but shows larger errors during the early transport stage, particularly under higher leachate heads where advective transport becomes more pronounced. The H-PINN reduces the optimization burden associated with penalty-based constraint enforcement and provides more accurate and stable concentration predictions, lowering the MAE from approximately 0.058-0.067 for the Std-PINN to about 0.011-0.023 for the H-PINN, while reducing the MRE from approximately 9.10%-19.16% to about 2.08%-3.14%. Parametric analyses confirm that the H-PINN with the tanh activation function and an optimized network structure provides the best predictive accuracy. The H-PINN is further extended to inverse modeling for identifying the SL degradation half-life from limited concentration observations, showing reliable convergence toward prescribed values and acceptable robustness under low-to-moderate observation noise.

### [286] [DPDL: Towards Differential Privacy Preservation in Decentralized Stochastic Learning on Non-IID Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04399)
*Yunsheng Yuan,Xue Xiao,Lina Wang,Feng Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种针对非独立同分布（non-IID）数据的隐私保护去中心化学习算法DPDL，通过基于相似性的校准技术结合差分隐私（DP）在跨梯度聚合中实现隐私保护。该方法在每轮中对邻居的局部模型在本地数据上的梯度进行高斯噪声扰动后共享，并利用余弦相似性校准接收到的噪声梯度，以实现类似动量的本地模型更新。理论分析表明，该算法在保证特定隐私水平的同时仍能实现线性加速训练；实验验证了其在抵御隐私攻击和训练高精度模型方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 去中心化学习虽能有效协作训练全局模型，但需频繁交换梯度信息，导致隐私泄露风险；同时真实场景中数据常为非独立同分布（non-IID），加剧了隐私保护与模型性能的挑战。因此亟需一种能在non-IID数据下实现隐私保护的去中心化学习方法。

Method: 提出DPDL算法，引入差分隐私机制，在跨梯度聚合时使用高斯噪声对每个代理的交叉梯度进行扰动；通过余弦相似性对收到的噪声梯度进行校准，使聚合后的梯度可被用于类似动量的方式更新本地模型。

Result: 理论分析揭示了实现特定隐私水平所需的最小噪声强度；证明算法在non-IID数据下仍能保持线性训练加速。大量实验证明：该算法在保护隐私、抵御隐私攻击方面表现优异，同时能训练出高精度模型。

Conclusion: DPDL是一种有效的隐私保护去中心化学习框架，适用于non-IID数据场景，在保障隐私的同时维持高效且准确的模型训练。

Abstract: In the paradigm of decentralized learning, a group of agents collaborate to train a global model using distributed datasets without a central server. Although the power of collaboration has been verified by many state-of-the-art studies, it entails extensive gradient information exchanging among the agents and thus induces high risk of privacy leakage for the individual agents. Moreover, in real-world applications, the training data are usually non-identically and independently distributed across the agents, inducing more challenges to enable privacy-preserved decentralized learning. To address these issues, we propose a privacy-preserved decentralized learning algorithm with non-IID data, DPDL, which leverages the notion of Differential Privacy (DP) in cross-gradient aggregation through a similarity-based calibration technique. Specifically, in each round, each agent perturbs the cross-gradients (i.e., the derivatives of its neighbors' local model in its private local data) by Gaussian noise mechanism before sharing them with its neighbors; it then adopt cosine similarity to calibrate the received perturbed cross-gradients such that the aggregation of the calibrated cross-gradients can be utilized to effectively update local model in a momentum-like manner. Our rigorous theoretical analysis not only reveals the minimum noise level required to achieve a specific level of privacy preservation, but also illustrates that our algorithm still achieves a linear speedup in training with non-IID data. We finally conduct extensive experiments on real-world dataset to validate the effectiveness of our algorithm in defending privacy attacks and in training accurate models.

</details>

Method: 将双层优化问题简化为单层惩罚形式，采用双网络结构：一个基于主要数据训练的代理模型和一个随额外数据动态更新的参考模型。通过比较两模型之间的差异来评估各领域的数据效用，并据此调整权重。

Abstract: The capabilities of large language models (LLMs) significantly depend on training data drawn from various domains. Our proposed method, Twin Networks for bi-level DatA mixturE optiMization (TANDEM), measures the data efficacy through the difference between the twin models and up-weights domains that benefit more from the additional data. TANDEM provides theoretical guarantees and wider applicability, compared to prior approaches. Furthermore, our bi-level perspective suggests new settings to study domain reweighting such as data-restricted scenarios and supervised fine-tuning, where optimized mixture ratios significantly improve the performance. Extensive experiments validate TANDEM's effectiveness in all scenarios.

### [288] [Low-Rank Decay for Grokking in Scale-Invariant Transformers: A Spectral-Geometric View](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04405)
*Mingyu Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在归一化Transformer架构中，标准权重衰减在尺度不变性下的局限性，并提出低秩衰减（LRD）作为一种基于核范数的谱正则化方法。LRD通过保留权重空间中的切向分量，在模型记忆训练集后仍能继续压缩奇异值，从而加速有效秩坍缩并促进延迟泛化（grokking）。实验表明，LRD在模运算任务中显著扩展了发生grokking的数据分数边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的Frobenius范数权重衰减在尺度不变的归一化模型中仅沿径向作用，无法改变模型函数表示；因此需要一种能在归一化后仍具有切向调节能力的正则化方法，以促进更有效的泛化行为，尤其是在延迟泛化（grokking）场景中。

Method: 提出低秩衰减（Low-Rank Decay, LRD），其子梯度为极分解中的$UV^\top$，保留了切向成分；通过分析权重谱动态，揭示了在任务梯度消失后，LRD仍能以类似$\ell_1$的方式压缩奇异值，而标准L2衰减失效。

Result: 在模运算任务中，使用LRD的模型实现了更快的有效秩坍缩，显著提升了查询/键矩阵的谱压缩效果，并将延迟泛化发生的最小数据分数边界大幅扩展。此外，提供了基于谱几何的解释：核范数次微分在低秩流形附近呈现“针到扇”的扩张特性。

Conclusion: LRD作为一种切向谱正则化方法，克服了传统权重衰减在尺度不变设置下的局限性，有效促进了深度学习模型中的延迟泛化现象，揭示了谱结构与泛化之间的深层联系。

Abstract: Modern Transformer architectures frequently employ normalization mechanisms such as RMSNorm and Query-Key Normalization, making parts of the model approximately scale-invariant with respect to weight magnitudes. In this regime, standard Frobenius-norm weight decay acts purely along the radial direction of the weight space and cannot directly simplify the function represented by the normalized layer. We study grokking in small algorithmic tasks through this lens and propose \emph{Low-Rank Decay} (LRD), a nuclear-norm-like spectral regularizer whose subgradient -- the polar factor $UV^\top$ -- retains a tangential component even in the scale-invariant setting. This distinction has a concrete dynamical consequence: after the model memorizes the training set and task gradients vanish, L2 decay can no longer reshape the weight spectrum, whereas LRD continues to compress singular values in an $\ell_1$-like fashion. On modular arithmetic tasks, we find that LRD induces rapid effective-rank collapse in Query/Key matrices and expands the data-fraction boundary at which delayed generalization (grokking) occurs. We further provide a spectral-geometric interpretation through the ``needle-to-fan'' expansion of the nuclear-norm subdifferential near low-rank strata.

By leveraging the complementary advantages of both optimization paradigms, ELFM-DEGDO is able to produce more comprehensive and less biased representations for HDI data. Three HDI datasets are tested to show that ELFM-DEGDO consistently performs better than related several latent factor models.

### [291] [Loss-Conditional PINNs for Parametric PDE Families](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04420)
*Anna Lazareva,Alexander Tarakanov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LC-PINN introduces a loss-conditional training approach for physics-informed neural networks (PINNs), enabling the model to learn a continuous family of solutions across varying loss weights or physical parameters without requiring retraining for each case. By treating loss weights or physical coefficients as input variables and sampling them during training, LC-PINN unifies both regimes under one architecture—using concatenation for weights and FiLM for coefficients—and employs a fixed-quadrature L-BFGS optimization protocol to improve training stability. The method achieves better or comparable performance than per-weight retrained PINNs while significantly reducing computational cost through amortized learning.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing PINNs suffer from poor performance due to sensitive loss weight choices, often leading to degenerate solutions where only one physical constraint is satisfied. Current methods focus on tuning a single optimal weight vector, but this limits adaptability. The motivation is to explore the full weight space during training to achieve robust, generalizable solutions across diverse physical conditions without repeated retraining.

Method: LC-PINN extends loss-conditional training by incorporating loss weights or physical parameters as inputs to the neural network. At each optimization step, these conditioning vectors are sampled from a prior distribution. The architecture uses concatenation for loss weights and Feature-wise Linear Modulation (FiLM) for physical coefficients. A fixed-quadrature L-BFGS finishing protocol ensures convergence and improves solution quality in the parametric-coefficient regime.

Result: LC-PINN matches or outperforms retrained PINN baselines across multiple benchmark PDEs including Helmholtz, Schrödinger, viscous Burgers, and Buckley-Leverett equations. It successfully parameterizes an entire family of solutions within a single model, achieving significant computational savings by amortizing training costs over the parameter space.

Conclusion: LC-PINN provides a unified, efficient framework for learning parametric families of PDE solutions without retraining. By exploring the full weight and parameter space through conditional training, it enhances robustness and generalization beyond traditional PINNs, offering a scalable alternative for physics-informed machine learning.

Abstract: Physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) approximate solutions of ODEs and PDEs by minimising a weighted combination of residual, boundary, initial, and data losses. Their performance is often dominated by the choice of loss weights: a poor weighting can drive training to a degenerate solution in which one physical constraint is satisfied while another is ignored. Existing methods select or adapt a single good set of weights. We take a different view: instead of tuning one weight vector, we explore the entire weight space during training.
  We introduce LC-PINN, which adapts the loss-conditional training of Dosovitskiy and Djolonga (2020) to the PDE-residual setting: the conditioning vector (either the loss weights or a scalar physical coefficient) is treated as a network input and sampled from a simple prior at every optimisation step. This turns PINN training into learning a continuous family of solutions indexed by that vector, with no solver-generated paired data. LC-PINN thus lies between classical PINNs and operator learning: it stays fully physics-informed but amortises training over a parametric family. Our contribution is not the loss-conditional construction itself, but its extension to PINNs, the unification of the loss-weight and parametric-coefficient regimes under one architecture (concatenation for loss weights, FiLM for coefficients), and a fixed-quadrature L-BFGS finishing protocol that makes the parametric-coefficient regime trainable.
  We give a lambda-invariance result for the conditional optimum and study LC-PINN on parametric Helmholtz, Schrodinger, viscous Burgers, and Buckley-Leverett equations. A single LC-PINN matches or improves retrained per-weight PINN baselines while parameterising the full family in one model, at a total cost that amortises favourably against per-instance retraining.

</details>


### [292] [The price of multi-group transductive learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04423)
*Noah Bergam,Samuel Deng,Daniel Hsu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 多组学习在归纳设置中可能在某些组上导致误差率的乘法惩罚，该惩罚随组数线性增长，最多可达样本量的平方根。这与在类似（组可实现）统计设置中表现最优的多组学习者形成鲜明对比，后者惩罚最多为样本量的对数级且与组数无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究多组学习在不同设置下的性能差异，揭示归纳设置中潜在的误差放大问题。

Method: 通过理论分析和构造反例，比较多组学习在归纳与统计设置中的误差行为。

Result: 在归纳设置中，多组学习者的误差率惩罚可能随组数线性增长，最大可达样本量的平方根；而在统计设置中，惩罚仅对数级且独立于组数。

Conclusion: 多组学习在归纳设置中存在严重的组间误差放大风险，而统计设置下则无此问题，表明设置选择对多组学习性能至关重要。

Abstract: We show every multi-group learner in the transductive setting may incur a multiplicative penalty in its error rate on some group relative to the error rate achievable in the single-group setting, and the penalty can increasing linearly with the number of groups, up to roughly the square-root of the sample size. This stands in stark contrast to optimal multi-group learners in an analogous (group-realizable) statistical setting, where the penalty is always at most logarithmic in the sample size and independent of the number of groups.

</details>


### [293] [LoopMoE: Unifying Iterative Computation with Mixture-of-Experts for Language Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04438)
*Wenkai Chen,Tianshu Li,Wenyong Huang,Yichun Yin,Lifeng Shang,Chengwei Qin*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 LoopMoE，采用 IterAdaLN 实现基于迭代索引和每标记隐藏状态的调制信号以打破权值共享对称性，并引入容量平衡策略恢复注意力到前馈网络活跃参数比例，从而实现严格可控的对比实验。

Conclusion: LoopMoE 成功实现了稀疏性与循环性的受控融合，验证了循环架构在语言模型中的有效性，为未来循环语言模型的发展提供了有力支持。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) and looped architectures scale models along two orthogonal axes, namely parameter capacity and effective depth. However, mainstream looped architectures rely on dense backbones that couple parameter count with per-token FLOPs, which makes it impossible to isolate the effect of iterative computation under matched budgets. To this end, we present LoopMoE, a looped MoE language model that integrates sparse routing with iterative weight-shared computation through two designs. The first is IterAdaLN, which resolves weight-sharing symmetry via a modulation signal jointly conditioned on the iteration index and the per-token hidden state. The second is a capacity-balancing strategy that recovers the attention-to-FFN active parameter ratio of well-tuned non-looped references. Together, these designs enable the first strictly controlled, head-to-head evaluation of a looped MoE against a Vanilla MoE under identical total parameters, per-token FLOPs, and active sublayer ratios. At the 3B scale, LoopMoE outperforms the Vanilla MoE on 8 of 9 downstream benchmarks with an average improvement exceeding 1 point. At the 9B scale, LoopMoE continues to outperform the matched Vanilla MoE, indicating that the architectural gain persists at larger scale. Our work establishes a controlled synthesis of sparsity and recurrence, and suggests a promising direction for looped language models.

Abstract: Real estate valuation is a structured regression problem in which prices are governed by heterogeneous feature types, sparse regional effects, nonlinear interactions, and the practical logic of comparable properties. Standard multilayer perceptrons treat each row as an isolated vector and must learn locality, scale sensitivity, and categorical matching from supervision alone. Gradient-boosted decision trees provide strong tabular baselines, but their feature-centric splitting mechanism does not explicitly model the retrieval of similar historical observations.
  This paper presents RowNet, a retrieval-based neural architecture for real estate price-per-square-meter prediction. RowNet represents a query property through pairwise similarity features against a memory bank of labeled properties. A first retrieval layer estimates a coarse target from feature-only similarities. A second layer augments the memory comparison with target-consistency features and uses multiple learned attention heads to retrieve complementary comparable sets. A final mixture-of-experts module combines learned gating, residual correction, entropy regularization, and head-diversity regularization to produce the prediction.

### [295] [On Out-of-sample Embedding in UMAP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04451)
*Mohammad Tariqul Islam,Jason W. Fleischer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种改进的UMAP算法，通过优化原始k近邻图中的成对交互来克服传统UMAP在处理新样本时的“排斥效应”，即新点常被放置在聚类外围而非内部。研究发现参数化UMAP能生成更优嵌入，尤其在复杂数据（如医学图像）上表现更佳，并自然缓解排斥效应。通过可信度、最近邻分类器及嵌入中吸引/排斥力分析，验证了不同方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统UMAP在添加新样本时存在排斥效应，导致新点被置于聚类外围而非与相关邻居聚集于内部，影响嵌入质量；需改进以提升外推能力。

Method: 通过优化原始k近邻图中的成对交互关系，引入参数化机制改进UMAP，使其能够更好地将新样本嵌入已有结构中，并通过吸引/排斥力分析和多种评估指标进行验证。

Result: 参数化UMAP显著减轻了排斥效应，在复杂数据（如医学图像）上优于非参数方法，且在可信度和分类性能方面表现更优。

Conclusion: 通过参数化设计和成对交互优化，可有效缓解UMAP的排斥效应，提升其在高维数据外推任务中的鲁棒性和准确性，尤其适用于复杂数据场景。

Abstract: Neighbor embedding algorithms reveal correlations in high-dimensional data by constructing an equivalent graph representation in a lower-dimensional space. An increasingly popular algorithm is Uniform Manifold Learning and Projection (UMAP), which uses algebraic topology to map distances between the two spaces. While it works well on many types of data sets, UMAP has trouble adding out-of-sample points to a pre-existing mapping. In particular, UMAP often places new points on the periphery of the found clusters, rather than in their interiors with their correlated neighbors. Here, we overcome this ``repulsion effect'' by optimizing pairwise interactions within the original k-nearest-neighbor graph. Moreover, we show that parameterizing UMAP obtains better embeddings than non-parametric algorithms, particularly as the data gets more complex (e.g., medical images). We also show that the repulsion effect is naturally mitigated when a parameterized UMAP is employed to embed the data. We characterize different UMAP approaches using trustworthiness, nearest neighbor classifiers, and by analyzing attractive and repulsive forces in the embeddings.

### [296] [ParetoPilot: Zero-Surrogate Offline Multi-Objective Optimization via Infer-Perturb-Guide Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04468)
*Ruiqing Sun,Sen Yang,Dawei Feng,Bo Ding,Yijie Wang,Huaimin Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ParetoPilot提出了一种无需代理模型的扩散框架，用于离线多目标优化。通过在反向生成过程中嵌入Infer-Perturb-Guide（IPG）引擎，利用预训练扩散模型中的条件先验，实现对目标方向的隐式推断与动态扰动，从而引导生成过程。该方法避免了外部代理模型带来的计算开销和评估偏差，显著提升帕累托前沿覆盖和超体积表现，在51个任务中优于14个先进基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成方法依赖外部代理模型，导致计算开销大、评估易受误导，并违背主流生成模型联合训练的范式。因此亟需一种无需代理模型、能高效生成帕累托最优解的离线多目标优化方法。

Method: 提出ParetoPilot框架，核心为Infer-Perturb-Guide（IPG）引擎，包含三步：1）通过匹配条件与无条件噪声预测，隐式推断目标方向；2）构建正交重力场以保证收敛性，以及边缘感知排斥力以增强多样性；3）生成动态退火扰动向量，并通过标准分类器无关引导（CFG）引导生成过程。

Result: 在51个任务上全面超越14个基于代理模型和逆向生成的先进基线方法，在帕累托前沿覆盖率和超体积指标上均有显著提升，且无需额外代理模型训练，保护数据隐私。

Conclusion: ParetoPilot是一种高效的零代理扩散框架，能够充分利用预训练扩散模型的内在条件先验，实现高质量离线多目标优化，为无需外部代理模型的生成式优化提供了新范式。

Abstract: Offline multi-objective optimization (Offline MOO) aims to discover novel Pareto-optimal designs based on static datasets without expensive environment interactions. While recent generative methods have achieved notable success, they predominantly rely on external surrogate models. This dependency introduces significant computational overhead, suffers from deceptive evaluations, and deviates from the prevailing paradigm of jointly training mainstream generative models with conditions. To address these bottlenecks, we propose ParetoPilot, a novel zero-surrogate diffusion framework for offline MOO. ParetoPilot fully leverages the conditional priors inherently embedded within pre-trained diffusion models. At its core, the framework introduces the Infer-Perturb-Guide (IPG) engine, which is seamlessly interleaved within the unconditional denoising steps of the reverse generation process. First, it implicitly infers the instantaneous objective direction by matching conditional and unconditional noise predictions. Next, it mathematically orthogonalizes a parallel gravity field for strict convergence and an edgeness-aware repulsive force for mutual diversity, creating a dynamically annealed perturbation vector. Finally, this perturbed target seamlessly steers the generation process via standard Classifier-Free Guidance (CFG). Extensive experiments across 51 tasks demonstrate that ParetoPilot outperforms 14 state-of-the-art surrogate-based and inverse generative baselines. By eliminating auxiliary proxy training, our approach preserves data privacy while achieving hypervolume improvement and robust Pareto front coverage.

### [298] [When Both Layers Learn: Training Dynamics of Representing Linear Models via ReLU Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04476)
*Berk Tinaz,Changzhi Xie,Mahdi Soltanolkotabi*

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维隐藏层ReLU网络在拟合线性目标函数时，联合训练两层的梯度下降动态。在输入服从高斯分布且标签符合预设线性模型的理想设定下，证明了从适度小的随机初始化出发，联合训练两层的梯度下降能以线性速率收敛到全局最小值，达到阶次最优的样本复杂度。分析揭示了三个阶段：对齐阶段、增长阶段和局部精炼阶段，并通过轨迹级控制与新型统一浓度不等式，严格证明了算法避免非严格鞍点的能力。实验验证了理论结果的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In this paper, we study the gradient descent dynamics for jointly training both layers of a one-hidden-layer ReLU network to fit a linear target function. Concretely, we consider a realizable setting where inputs are drawn i.i.d. from a Gaussian distribution and labels follow a planted linear model. This stylized framework captures salient features of end-to-end training in inverse problems and certain auto-encoder models. Despite its apparent simplicity, the dynamics remain poorly understood, in part because the loss landscape contains multiple non-strict saddle points, making it unclear why gradient descent from random initialization reliably escapes bad stationary regions. We provide a detailed characterization of the optimization landscape and prove that gradient descent from a moderately small random initialization-simultaneously training both layers-converges to a global minimizer at a linear rate with order-wise optimal sample complexity. Our analysis tracks the trajectory through three phases: an alignment phase in which hidden weights progressively align with the planted direction while the output weights maintain the correct sign pattern; a growth phase in which the norms of both layers increase while preserving alignment; and a local refinement phase in which the aligned neurons rapidly converge to the planted direction, yielding fast local convergence. To rigorously show that GD avoids non-strict saddles, we develop trajectory-level control arguments for the end-to-end dynamics. In addition, we establish novel uniform concentration results that hold along the entire trajectory, and are essential for obtaining order-wise optimal sample complexity. We corroborate our theory with extensive experiments across a range of configurations.

### [299] [LimiX-2M: Mitigating Low-Rank Collapse and Attention Bottlenecks in Tabular Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04485)
*Yuanrui Wang,Xingxuan Zhang,Han Yu,Mingchao Ming,Gang Ren,Hao Yuan,Li Mao,Yunjia Zhang,Chun Yuan,Peng Cui*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种统一的 tokenize-and-route 框架，通过 RaBEL 将标量特征转换为紧凑的局部 RBF 特征，并采用 S→N→F 顺序的双向块结构，提升浅层值敏感性和有效秩，从而构建出仅 2M 参数的 LimiX-2M 模型。该模型在多个基准测试中超越更大的 TabPFN-v2 和 TabICL，同时降低训练和推理成本，验证了值感知标记化与读出对齐路由的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有表格式基础模型（TFMs）在性能上虽接近树集成模型，但计算效率低下，主要因标准仿射标量标记化导致每个特征仅通过一维通道传递值变化，且特征 ID/位置信号无法增加特征内值的自由度，造成浅层值敏感性弱和隐藏状态冗余。

Method: 提出 RaBEL 方法，将每个标量扩展为紧凑的局部径向基函数（RBF）特征（可选指数门控），以增强条件建模和浅层有效秩；设计 S→N→F 重排的双向块结构，先聚合跨样本上下文再进行特征混合，并使用注意力池化，使计算更符合读出需求。

Result: 构建的 LimiX-2M 模型（仅 200 万参数）在多个主流表格数据集上优于更大的 TabPFN-v2 与 TabICL 基线，同时显著降低训练和推理开销，证明了值感知标记化与读出对齐路由对提升准确率-效率权衡的关键作用。

Conclusion: 值感知标记化与读出对齐路由是提升表格式基础模型准确性与效率的核心机制，本研究提出的框架为高效强健的表格式模型设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Tabular foundation models (TFMs) increasingly rival tree ensembles, but their performance is often compute-inefficient: with standard affine scalar tokenization, each feature injects value variation through an essentially one-dimensional channel, and feature IDs/positional signals cannot increase within-feature value degrees of freedom, yielding weak early-layer value sensitivity and redundant hidden states. We present a unified \emph{tokenize-and-route} framework for strong TFMs: \textbf{RaBEL} expands each scalar into compact localized RBF features (optionally exponent-gated) to improve conditioning and shallow-layer effective rank, while a reordered bidirectional block \textbf{S$\rightarrow$N$\rightarrow$F} aligns computation with the readout by aggregating cross-sample context before feature mixing and using attention pooling. Together, these changes yield \textbf{LimiX-2M}, a 2M-parameter model that outperforms larger TabPFN-v2 and TabICL baselines on widely used tabular benchmarks while reducing training and inference costs. These results highlight value-aware tokenization and readout-aligned routing as key levers for improving the accuracy--efficiency trade-off in TFMs. Model checkpoints and inference code are available at https://github.com/limix-ldm-ai/LimiX.

### [300] [Episodic Memory Temporal Consistency for Cooperative Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04492)
*Zicheng Zhao,Yu Lan,Chengzhengxu Li,Zhaohan Zhang,Xiaoming Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出EMTC框架，通过时间一致性语义嵌入和时序一致性门控机制，解决多智能体强化学习中的奖励稀疏与探索瓶颈问题，有效防止表征崩溃并过滤误导性信号，理论证明其误差边界，并在SMAC和GRF基准上显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统协作式多智能体强化学习面临奖励稀疏和探索困难，尽管利用情景记忆可重用高回报轨迹，但易陷入局部最优，因激励分配无约束和语义表征崩溃。

Method: 提出双组件框架EMTC：(1) 时间一致语义嵌入器，结合对比学习与时间条件状态重建，防止表征崩溃；(2) 时序一致性门控机制，基于时序一致性误差动态调节情景激励，过滤伪成功轨迹的误导信号。

Result: 在SMAC和GRF基准上显著优于现有方法，相比最强基线，在超难SMAC场景中最高提升24%胜率，GRF任务平均提升28%。

Conclusion: EMTC通过时间一致性机制实现更稳健的记忆构建与选择性利用，有效缓解多智能体强化学习中的关键挑战，具备理论保障与实证优势。

Abstract: Cooperative Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) frequently suffers from severe reward sparsity and exploration bottlenecks. While episodic memory mechanisms mitigate these issues by reusing high-return trajectories, they often trap agents in local optima due to unconstrained incentive distribution and semantic representation collapse. To address this, we propose Episodic Memory Temporal Consistency (EMTC), a framework that robustly constructs and selectively leverages historical experiences. EMTC introduces two synergistic components: (1) a Temporally Consistent Semantic Embedder that integrates contrastive learning with time-conditioned state reconstruction, preventing representation collapse and enabling precise memory retrieval; and (2) a Temporal Consistency Gating Mechanism that dynamically modulates episodic incentives based on temporal consistency error. This adaptive gate filters misleading signals from pseudo-successful trajectories, effectively mitigating Q-value overestimation. We provide theoretical guarantees, establishing a strict error bound that directly links the observable temporal consistency error to the underlying trajectory optimality and representation quality. Extensive evaluations on the SMAC and GRF benchmarks demonstrate that EMTC consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines. Notably, compared to the strongest episodic baseline, EMTC achieves absolute win-rate improvements of up to 24% in super-hard SMAC scenarios and an average improvement of 28% across GRF tasks.

### [301] [Smart Picks in the Dark: Towards Efficient RLVR for Reasoning via Tracing Metacognitive Pivots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04503)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习带可验证奖励（RLVR）方法依赖大量标注数据，数据选择方法需预先有标注数据池，而无监督方法性能不佳。因此，亟需一种无需先验监督即可挑选对训练最有价值的未标注样本的方法，以提升数据效率和训练效率。

Method: 提出PivotTrace三路数据筛选框架，利用注意力机制追踪推理过程中的元认知枢纽，基于枢纽密度构建校准的不确定性估计，实现对未标注数据的智能分区与自适应训练策略。

Conclusion: PivotTrace通过精准的不确定性估计与智能数据路由，有效解决了无监督环境下数据筛选难题，为高效、低成本训练大推理模型提供了新路径。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has greatly advanced large reasoning models (LRMs), but it requires timely training on a huge fully-annotated dataset. To this end, data-efficient RLVR methods have been widely studied from two perspectives: (i) data selection methods identify a small subset of "golden" samples that yield near-full-data performance, but they rely on a pre-existing pool of labeled data. (ii) unsupervised RLVR methods train the model using its own internal supervision signals on large-scale unlabeled data, yet they exhibit suboptimal performance. Accordingly, we investigate the "pick in the dark" setup for RLVR, which aims to select, without prior supervision, unlabeled samples that are most beneficial for training and worthy of annotation. Through systematic analysis, we demonstrate that smart picks hinge on a well-calibrated uncertainty estimator to enable strategic partitioning of data for adaptive training regimes. Building on this insight, we propose PivotTrace, a three-way data triage framework that leverages attention dynamics to trace metacognitive pivots during reasoning. By precisely quantifying uncertainty through pivot density, PivotTrace achieves automated data routing to synergistically maximize both annotation and training efficiency. Empirically, PivotTrace surpasses the fully supervised LRM with only 29.3% annotated samples and 2.75 faster convergence.

To this end, we propose GeoMin, which models global feature distributions on labeled data to decode the structural discrepancy between correct and incorrect rollouts, thereby establishing a robust prior to assess the reliability of self-reward signals and fully unleash the potential of unlabeled data. Empirically, GeoMin outperforms the strongest baselines by +4.1% and even surpasses fully supervised models with only 10% of the annotations, demonstrating remarkable data efficiency.

### [303] [Rollout-Level Advantage-Prioritized Experience Replay for GRPO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04560)
*Gyeongtae Yoo,Sanghyeok Park,Soohyuk Jang,Ik-hwan Kim,Sungroh Yoon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种针对GRPO的基于回放的强化学习方法，通过存储和采样单个推理轨迹（rollout）而非整组数据，结合年龄淘汰机制和新鲜锚定组合策略，有效缓解了大模型政策快速漂移导致的轨迹过时问题。在多个数学基准测试中，该方法显著优于GRPO和朴素回放基线，尤其在4B模型规模下表现最佳，平均准确率提升4.35个百分点，并在综合精度与效率指标（AES）上领先0.579。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于可验证奖励的强化学习（GRPO）在后训练推理大模型时存在样本效率低的问题，每次推演仅用于一次梯度更新即被丢弃；而传统回放方式因大模型策略快速变化导致存储轨迹迅速过时，难以稳定训练。因此需要一种能有效管理轨迹新鲜度并保留高价值信息的新回放机制。

Method: 提出一种轨迹级回放缓冲区，以个体推演为单位进行存储与采样；通过设定最大年龄阈值（tau_max）实现过时轨迹的自动剔除；采用‘新鲜锚定’策略，在每批次中保留新生成的在线轨迹，再独立从缓冲区中采样回放轨迹，并按每个推演的优势大小进行优先级排序，对高优势推演进行重复利用。

Result: 在三个Qwen3-Base模型规模（不同尺寸）上，五个数学基准测试中，所提方法均优于GRPO和朴素回放基线，且性能增益随模型规模增大而提升。最大提升达+4.35个百分点（5基准平均），在AES指标下，4B模型的效率优势最大，达到+0.579。

Conclusion: 所提出的轨迹级回放机制有效解决了大模型强化学习中轨迹过时与样本效率低的问题，通过合理控制轨迹新鲜度与优先重用高价值推演，显著提升了训练稳定性与性能，尤其在大规模模型上展现出更强优势。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards with GRPO is a standard approach for post-training reasoning LLMs. It remains sample inefficient. Each rollout is used for a single gradient update and then discarded. Naive replay is not well suited in this setting because LLM policies drift quickly per gradient step. Stored rollouts therefore become stale and can destabilize training. We propose a rollout-level replay buffer for GRPO that stores and samples individual rollouts rather than whole groups. The buffer bounds staleness through age eviction. Any rollout older than tau_max training steps is removed. The buffer also preserves on-policy data via fresh-anchored composition. Each batch keeps its fresh on-policy rollouts and then concatenates replay rollouts drawn separately from the buffer. We prioritize replay by per-rollout advantage magnitude and recycle individual rollouts whose advantages are large. Across three Qwen3-Base scales on five math benchmarks, our method outperforms GRPO and naive replay baselines. Gains are positive at every scale and grow with model size. The largest gain is +4.35 pp on the five-benchmark average at 4B. Under an AES metric that jointly measures accuracy and token efficiency, the efficiency margin over GRPO is again largest at 4B, at +0.579.

</details>


### [304] [SurvPFN: Towards Foundation Models for Survival Predictions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04564)
*Samuel Böhm,Lennart Purucker,Frank Hutter,Pascal Schlosser*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出SurvPFN，一种用于生存预测的先验数据拟合网络（PFN），通过在数百万个合成生存任务上预训练，学习考虑删失数据的分布回归，以解决标准表格基础模型无法原生处理删失数据的问题。SurvPFN通过生成威布尔事件时间、整合删失事件指示器并最小化删失负对数似然来实现。在SurvSet真实世界生存任务上，SurvPFN表现出色，无需特定数据集微调、专用架构或特征工程即可媲美经典和深度生存基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准表格基础模型无法原生处理删失数据，导致生存预测中出现偏差和不准确，限制了其在现实应用中的使用。因此需要一种能有效处理删失数据的新型模型。

Method: 在合成数据上预训练SurvPFN，采用威布尔分布生成事件时间，引入非信息性删失机制，结合删失事件指示符，并通过最小化删失负对数似然进行优化，将生存预测建模为连续时间的分布回归问题。

Result: SurvPFN在SurvSet数据集上表现优异，无需针对具体数据集进行微调、特殊架构或特征工程，性能可与经典和深度生存模型相媲美，验证了其通用性和有效性。

Conclusion: 生存预测可被建模为考虑删失数据的连续时间分布回归问题，利用PFNs能够有效解锁其在时间-事件预测中的潜力，为生存分析提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Tabular foundation models (TFMs) have made rapid progress in standard classification and regression, but time-to-event survival prediction tasks have remained largely untouched. Unlike in standard regression tasks, survival prediction models must account for censored data. Standard TFMs cannot handle natively censored data, leading to biased and inaccurate predictions, making them unsuitable for real-world applications. To overcome this fundamental limitation, we propose \texttt{SurvPFN}, a prior-data fitted network (PFN), for survival prediction tasks. We pretrain \texttt{SurvPFN} on millions of synthetic survival prediction tasks to learn survival via distributional regression that accounts for censored data. \texttt{SurvPFN} works by (1) generating data with Weibull event times and a non-informative censoring mechanism; (2) integrating a censored event indicator; and (3) minimizing a censored negative log-likelihood. On SurvSet, a collection of real-world survival tasks, \texttt{SurvPFN} is highly competitive with classical and deep survival baselines without per-dataset fitting, a survival-specific architecture, or feature engineering. We show that survival can be treated as a continuous-time distributional regression problem with censored loss, unlocking the power of PFNs for time-to-event predictions.

To address this need, this research introduces novel concepts. Although falling marginally short of the stricter 5 percent threshold, this result highlights the extreme idiosyncratic variance characteristic of digital assets. Ultimately, this thesis contributes to the quantitative finance literature by introducing a hybrid architecture that combines statistical arbitrage with DRL execution policies. Furthermore, it delivers a novel framework for safe reinforcement learning via deterministic shielding, proving that anchoring a neural policy to statistically robust boundaries successfully mitigates severe divergence risks.

### [306] [HalfNet: Randomized Neural Networks with Learned Subspace Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04583)
*Ethem Alpaydin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HalfNet proposes learning a low-rank covariance matrix $\Sigma$ for random weight initialization in neural networks, improving efficiency and performance by leveraging data-dependent geometry. It achieves competitive results on MNIST and CIFAR-10 with fewer parameters, demonstrating that predictive power stems more from weight space geometry than exact parameter values.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To improve the efficiency of neural networks by reducing parameters while maintaining performance, by learning a data-dependent structure for random weight initialization instead of using fixed distributions like $N(0, I)$.

Method: HalfNet initializes weights from $N(0, \Sigma)$, where $\Sigma$ is learned via low-rank factorization from data, enabling a data-driven random embedding that can be interpreted through metric learning, kernel, or random feature perspectives.

Result: HalfNet matches the performance of fully trained multilayer perceptrons on MNIST and CIFAR-10 while using significantly fewer parameters; accuracy increases smoothly with rank, indicating the importance of weight space geometry.

Conclusion: The success of HalfNet shows that the geometry of weight space is crucial for neural network performance, and learning a structured random initialization via low-rank $\Sigma$ offers an efficient and effective alternative to full training.

Abstract: Many researchers investigated neural networks with some of their weights fixed to values randomly drawn from a given distribution, e.g., $N(0, I)$. Our proposed HalfNet draws random weights from $N(0, Σ)$, where $Σ$, which defines the geometry of the distribution, has a low-rank factorization that we learn from data. Experiments on MNIST and CIFAR-10 demonstrate that HalfNet can match the performance of fully trained multilayer perceptrons while using substantially fewer parameters. Spectral analysis indicates that much of the predictive power of neural networks lies in the geometry of their weight space rather than in the precise values of individual parameters, and we observe that accuracy scales smoothly with rank. HalfNet is not a neural architecture trick for low-rank structure; it implements a data-dependent random embedding that can also be interpreted through supervised metric learning, or random-feature and kernel perspectives.

</details>


### [307] [QuBLAST: A Framework for Quantizing Large Language Models with Block-Level Compression Approach and Activation Scaling Strategy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04620)
*Pasindu Wickramasinghe,Achyuta Muthuvelan,Rachmad Vidya Wicaksana Putra,Minghao Shao,Muhammad Shafique*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出QuBLAST，一种针对LLM的新型后训练量化方法，通过块级压缩和激活缩放策略实现混合精度量化，有效降低模型大小40%-45.2%的同时保持性能损失在5%以内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法采用统一量化策略，忽略不同注意力块的敏感性差异；复杂操作带来高计算开销；未考虑非传统架构（如状态空间模型）的量化挑战。

Method: 基于交叉熵损失分析各注意力块敏感性，确定权重量化级别；为每个块设计激活缩放图以控制激活值范围，缓解异常值影响。

Result: 在Qwen3-8B、Llama3-8B、Mistral v0.1-8B和Falcon H1R-7B等模型上，模型尺寸减少40%-45.2%，在WikiText-2和WikiText-103数据集上困惑度增加不超过5%。

Conclusion: QuBLAST通过块级混合精度量化与高效激活缩放策略，显著降低部署成本，适用于多种主流及新兴架构的LLM，具有良好的实用性与扩展性。

Abstract: LLMs have become the state-of-the-art algorithms for solving NLP tasks. However, they typically come at huge computational and memory costs, thus making them difficult to deploy on embedded systems. Toward this, state-of-the-art methods typically employ uniform post-training quantization (PTQ) across attention blocks of the network, hence overlooking the potential of applying different quantization levels in the same network. They also employ complex operations to mitigate the negative impact of activation outliers, hence incurring high computational overheads. Moreover, they have not considered evaluation using emerging LLMs with non-conventional attention architectures (e.g., state-space models), which pose different challenges in applying quantization. To address these limitations, we propose QuBLAST, a novel PTQ methodology that employs block-level compression approach with activation scaling strategy for LLMs. Block-level compression approach enables mixed-precision quantization across blocks of the network, while activation scaling strategy efficiently mitigates the negative impact of activation outliers. Specifically, QuBLAST first analyzes the sensitivity of different attention blocks in the pre-trained model through the cross-entropy loss analysis. QuBLAST leverages this sensitivity analysis to determine the weight quantization level for each attention block in the model. Furthermore, QuBLAST employs the activation scaling map for each block to control the range of activation values and mitigate the negative impact of activation outliers, thereby enabling better quantization results. Experimental results show that, QuBLAST reduces model sizes by 40%-45.2% across different model architectures (i.e., Qwen3-8B, Llama3-8B, Mistral v0.1-8B, and Falcon H1R-7B), while maintaining the performance within 5% perplexity increase for the WikiText-2 and WikiText-103 datasets.

### [308] [Learning symplectic model reduction based on a approximation theorem of symplectic embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04623)
*Liyi Feng,Yifa Tang,Yulin Xie,Ruili Zhang,Aiqing Zhu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种保持辛结构的自编码器（SpAE），用于高维哈密顿系统的降维建模。通过建立辛嵌入的通用逼近定理，SpAE在构造上保证了辛结构的精确保留，使模型在长期预测中具有更高的稳定性与准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准自编码器在降维过程中容易破坏哈密顿系统的辛结构，导致长期预测不稳定，因此需要一种能够保持辛结构的神经网络方法。

Method: 基于辛嵌入的通用逼近定理，设计对称性保持的自编码器架构：解码器参数化为辛嵌入，编码器为对应的辛投影，通过无约束优化进行训练。

Result: 在高维格点和粒子系统上的实验表明，SpAE在重建精度和长期预测性能方面均显著优于传统方法。

Conclusion: 所提出的SpAE方法在保持辛结构的同时实现了高效且准确的模型降维，为高维哈密顿系统的数据驱动建模提供了可靠框架。

Abstract: High-dimensional Hamiltonian systems play a central role in many scientific and engineering disciplines, with dynamics evolving on symplectic manifolds. Although deep learning provides powerful tools for constructing low-dimensional surrogates from data, the intrinsic symplectic structure is easily destroyed during model reduction. As a result, a standard autoencoder may produce latent coordinates that do not support a Hamiltonian flow, leading to unstable long-time prediction. In this paper, we first establish a universal approximation theorem for symplectic embeddings. Based on this theory, we propose symplecticity-preserving autoencoders (SpAE), in which the decoder is parameterized as a symplectic embedding and the encoder is constructed as the corresponding symplectic projection. This architecture is expressive enough to approximate nonlinear symplectic embeddings and the associated symplectic projections, preserves the symplectic structure exactly by construction, and can be trained by standard unconstrained optimization, thereby improving both reconstruction and prediction accuracy. Extensive experiments on high-dimensional lattice and particle systems demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method.

Standard Reinforcement Learning (RL) methods also struggle with the adversarial trade-offs of critical care and often produce opaque policies with limited clinical interpretability. To address these limitations, we introduce VentAgent, a hierarchical framework in which Large Language Models (LLMs) act as transparent arbitrators for mechanical ventilation. We reformulate ventilation control as a dynamic Multi-Objective Arbitration process rather than single-objective optimization. VentAgent decomposes decision-making into three interpretable stages: Perception, Planning, and Orchestration. By leveraging the semantic reasoning capabilities of LLMs, it synthesizes strategies from heterogeneous experts and resolves conflicting clinical priorities through an explicit coordination mechanism. Evaluations on a high-fidelity physiological simulator show that VentAgent outperforms state-of-the-art RL and classical control baselines. Moreover, it converts control decisions into human-readable reasoning chains, offering a safer, more interpretable, and adaptable paradigm for critical care automation.

### [310] [Explainably Safe Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04634)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation:  learned systems in reinforcement learning often lack transparency, making it difficult for humans to trust their decisions. While shielding provides safety guarantees, its non-deterministic nature leads to complex, uninterpretable decision-making processes. Existing methods like decision trees struggle with the size and complexity of shielded policies, limiting explainability.

Method: Proposes a hierarchical decision tree framework to represent shielding policies. Uses a world model at design time to analyze action safety in different states, constructing high-level risk classification trees (safe, critical, dangerous, unsafe). At runtime, generates localized decision trees that explain allowed actions and why others are unsafe.

Result: Explanations generated via decision trees are several orders of magnitude smaller than the original shield, significantly improving interpretability. The method requires no additional data beyond what is used for shielding, incurs minimal computational overhead, and integrates smoothly into existing shielded RL pipelines.

Conclusion: The proposed approach enhances trust in safe reinforcement learning by providing human-interpretable explanations of shielded decisions through compact, hierarchical decision trees. Abstract: Trust in a decision-making system requires both safety guarantees and the ability to interpret and understand its behavior. This is particularly important for learned systems, whose decision-making processes are often highly opaque. Shielding is a prominent model-based technique for enforcing safety in reinforcement learning. However, because shields are automatically synthesized using rigorous formal methods, their decisions are often similarly difficult for humans to interpret. Recently, decision trees became customary to represent controllers and policies. However, since shields are inherently non-deterministic, their decision tree representations become too large to be explainable in practice. To address this challenge, we propose a novel approach for explainable safe RL that enhances trust by providing human-interpretable explanations of the shield's decisions. Our method represents the shielding policy as a hierarchy of decision trees, offering top-down, case-based explanations. At design time, we use a world model to analyze the safety risks of executing actions in given states. Based on this analysis, we construct both the shield and a high-level decision tree that classifies states into risk categories (safe, critical, dangerous, unsafe), explaining why a situation may be safety-critical. At runtime, we generate localized decision trees that explain which actions are allowed and why others are deemed unsafe. Our method facilitates explainability of the safety aspect in safe-by-shielding reinforcement learning, requires no additional information beyond what is already used for shielding, incurs minimal overhead, and integrates readily into existing shielded RL pipelines. In our experiments, we compute explanations using decision trees that are several orders of magnitude smaller than the original shield.

Abstract: Active learning (AL) for node classification typically focuses on selecting the most informative nodes for annotation within one or a few large graphs (e.g., in social network analysis). However, in other domains, such as molecular chemistry or electronic design automation, datasets consist of thousands of independent graphs. In many of these inductive settings, annotating an individual node requires a full-graph analysis, which effectively yields the remaining node labels on-the-fly. Therefore, these scenarios require AL strategies that select entire graphs instead of single nodes, a problem which has not been tackled in the literature so far. Thus, we introduce ALINC, an AL framework for inductive node classification via graph sampling. Our detailed analysis further reveals that the choice of the aggregation method is pivotal, as it substantially affects model performance and annotation costs. Finally, we demonstrate the effectiveness of ALINC in two use case studies: site-of-metabolism prediction in molecules and design automation of printed circuit board schematics.

### [312] [Why Muon Outperforms Adam: A Curvature Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04662)
*Shuche Wang,Fengzhuo Zhang,Jiaxiang Li,Dirk Bergemann,Zhuoran Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Muon outperforms Adam in training efficiency for large language models by achieving greater one-step loss reduction, primarily due to lower Normalized Directional Sharpness (NDS) rather than smaller update norms. This advantage stems from Muon's ability to better manage curvature penalties, especially under data imbalance and heterogeneous curvature, as shown through Taylor approximation, decomposition analysis, and theoretical proof on quadratic problems.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the local geometric origin of Muon's superior training efficiency over Adam in large language models, particularly focusing on curvature effects that are not yet well understood.

Method: The study uses second-order Taylor approximation of the training landscape, decomposes curvature penalty into update norm and NDS, analyzes data imbalance via Zipf-PCFG synthetic data, conducts within-/cross-layer curvature breakdown, and provides theoretical analysis on stylized quadratic problems with heterogeneous curvature and gradient alignment.

Result: Muon achieves a larger one-step loss decrease than Adam at equivalent validation loss; both optimizers have similar first-order gains but Muon incurs significantly smaller second-order curvature penalties due to lower NDS, not smaller updates. Data imbalance enhances Muon’s NDS advantage, and within-layer curvature plays a dominant role in the middle/late training stages. Theoretical results confirm Muon reduces average NDS compared to GD and achieves lower local quadratic loss under strong curvature heterogeneity.

Conclusion: Muon's training efficiency gain over Adam arises from its ability to minimize Normalized Directional Sharpness (NDS), which reflects a more favorable handling of local curvature. This is driven by effective balancing of update energy across curvature groups, particularly beneficial under data imbalance and heterogeneous curvature, offering a geometric explanation for its empirical success.

Abstract: Muon improves training efficiency over Adam in large language-model training by about two times, but the local geometric source of this advantage remains unclear. Our work takes a first step toward demystifying Muon's superiority over Adam from a curvature perspective. First, we apply a second-order Taylor approximation to the training landscape and show that Muon achieves a larger one-step loss decrease than Adam at matched validation loss. The two optimizers have comparable first-order gains, but Muon consistently incurs a smaller second-order curvature penalty. Second, we decompose this curvature penalty into the squared update norm and Normalized Directional Sharpness (NDS). We find that Muon and Adam have comparable update norms, so Muon's smaller curvature penalty is driven by lower NDS, not update scale. Third, we study how training data and model structure shape Muon's NDS advantage. Using Zipf-Probabilistic Context-Free Grammar (PCFG) data with controlled imbalance, we show that data imbalance amplifies Muon's NDS advantage over Adam. A within-/cross-layer decomposition further shows that, in the middle and late stages of training, Muon's lower NDS is mainly sustained by smaller within-layer curvature. Beyond empirical evidence, we analyze stylized quadratic problems with heterogeneous curvature and gradient alignment toward high-curvature modes. We prove that Muon attains a smaller average NDS than GD by balancing update energy across curvature groups; when curvature heterogeneity is sufficiently strong, this also yields lower local quadratic loss after the same number of steps.

*Yacouba Kaloga,Shashi Kumar,Shakeel A. Sheikh,Driss Khalil,Petr Motlicek,Ina Kodrasi*

Abstract: End-to-end ASR systems typically use fixed-depth acoustic encoders at inference, making it difficult to trade additional test-time computation for improved recognition without training a larger model. A natural approach is to reuse a shared Transformer block recurrently, but we find that naive looping does not fully exploit additional recurrent compute. We introduce LARM, a depth-conditioned looped Transformer that turns recurrent encoder depth into a controllable test-time compute axis. LARM combines sparse CTC checkpoints, supervision-clock embeddings, FiLM depth conditioning, and delayed soft-posterior feedback. These components structure the loop into recognition checkpoints separated by latent refinement phases and allow shared weights to specialize across recurrent steps. On LibriSpeech, LARM improves WER as the number of inference loops increases and achieves performance competitive with deeper unshared-parameter baselines. Our results show that test-time compute scaling can extend beyond autoregressive language-model reasoning to continuous non-autoregressive speech recognition.
